tvadbuddhibalam āśritya yāgārho smi janārdanad pītaṃ pṛthivyāṃ kruddhena yaśas te puruṣottamad jarāsaṃdhavadhenaiva prāptās te vipulāḥ śriyaḥd evaṃ saṃbhāṣya kaunteyaḥ prādād rathavaraṃ prabhod pratigṛhya tu govindo jarāsaṃdhasya taṃ rathamd prahṛṣṭas tasya mumude phalgunena janārdanaḥd prītimān abhavad rājan dharmarājapuraskṛtaḥa yathāvayaḥ samāgamya rājabhis taiś ca pāṇḍavaḥc satkṛtya pūjayitvā ca visasarja narādhipāna yudhiṣṭhirābhyanujñātās te nṛpā hṛṣṭamānasāḥc jagmuḥ svadeśāṃs tvaritā yānair uccāvacais tataḥa evaṃ puruṣaśārdūlo mahābuddhir janārdanaḥc pāṇḍavair ghātayām āsa jarāsaṃdham ariṃ tadāa ghātayitvā jarāsaṃdhaṃ buddhipūrvam ariṃdamaḥc dharmarājam anujñāpya pṛthāṃ kṛṣṇāṃ ca bhārataa subhadrāṃ bhīmasenaṃ ca phalgunaṃ yamajau tathāc dhaumyam āmantrayitvā ca prayayau svāṃ purīṃ pratid pāṇḍavair anudhāvadbhir yudhiṣṭhirapurogamaiḥd harṣeṇa mahatā yuktaḥ prāpya cānuttamaṃ yaśaḥd jagāma hṛṣṭaḥ kṛṣṇas tu punar dvāravatīṃ purīma tenaiva rathamukhyena taruṇādityavarcasāc dharmarājavisṛṣṭena divyenānādayan diśaḥa tato yudhiṣṭhiramukhāḥ pāṇḍavā bharatarṣabhac pradakṣiṇam akurvanta kṛṣṇam akliṣṭakāriṇama tato gate bhagavati kṛṣṇe devakinandanec jayaṃ labdhvā suvipulaṃ rājñām abhayadās tadāa saṃvardhitaujaso bhūyaḥ karmaṇā tena bhāratac draupadyāḥ pāṇḍavā rājan parāṃ prītim avardhayana tasmin kāle tu yad yuktaṃ dharmakāmārthasaṃhitamc tad rājā dharmataś cakre rājyapālanakīrtimān vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa pārthaḥ prāpya dhanuḥśreṣṭham akṣayyau ca maheṣudhīc rathaṃ dhvajaṃ sabhāṃ caiva yudhiṣṭhiram abhāṣatad ṛṣes tad vacanaṃ cintya niśaśvāsa yudhiṣṭhiraḥd dharmaṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ kartum icchan paraṃtapaḥd tasyeṅgitajño bībhatsuḥ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥd saṃvivartayiṣuḥ kāmaṃ pāvakāt pākaśāsaniḥa dhanur astraṃ śarā vīryaṃ pakṣo bhūmir yaśo balamc prāptam etan mayā rājan duṣprāpaṃ yad abhīpsitamd etac chrutvā kuruśreṣṭho dharmarājaḥ sahānujaḥd prahṛṣṭo mantribhiś caiva vyāsadhaumyādibhiḥ sahad tato vyāso mahābuddhir uvācedaṃ vaco rjunamd sādhu sādhv iti kaunteya diṣṭyā te buddhir īdṛśīd pṛthivīm akhilāṃ jetum eko vyavasito bhavānd dhanyaḥ pāṇḍur mahīpālo yasya putras tvam īdṛśaḥd sarvaṃ prāpsyati rājendro dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥd tvadvīryeṇa sa dharmātmā sārvabhaumatvam eṣyatid tvadbāhubalam āśritya rājasūyam avāpsyatid sunayād vāsudevasya bhīmārjunabalena cad yamayoś caiva vīryeṇa sarvaṃ prāpsyati dharmarāṭd tasmād diśaṃ devaguptām udīcīṃ gaccha phalgunad śakto bhavān surāñ jitvā ratnāny āhartum ojasād prācīṃ bhīmo balaślāghī prayātu bharatarṣabhad yāmyāṃ tatra diśaṃ yātu sahadevo mahārathaḥd pratīcīṃ nakulo gantā varuṇenābhipālitāmd eṣā me naiṣṭhikī buddhiḥ kriyatāṃ bharatarṣabhāḥd śrutvā vyāsavaco hṛṣṭās tam ūcuḥ pāṇḍunandanāḥd evam astu muniśreṣṭha yathājñāpayasi prabhod te py anujñāpya rājānaṃ sainyena mahatā vṛtāḥa tatra kṛtyam ahaṃ manye kośasyāsya vivardhanamc karam āhārayiṣyāmi rājñaḥ sarvān nṛpottamaa vijayāya prayāsyāmi diśaṃ dhanadarakṣitāmb sarve vāyupravegāś ca sarvālaṃkārabhūṣitāḥc tithāv atha muhūrte ca nakṣatre ca tathā śivea dhanaṃjayavacaḥ śrutvā dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥc snigdhagambhīranādinyā taṃ girā pratyabhāṣataa svasti vācyārhato viprān prayāhi bharatarṣabhac durhṛdām apraharṣāya suhṛdāṃ nandanāya cae vijayas te dhruvaṃ pārtha priyaṃ kāmam avāpnuhia ity uktaḥ prayayau pārthaḥ sainyena mahatā vṛtaḥc agnidattena divyena rathenādbhutakarmaṇāa tathaiva bhīmaseno pi yamau ca puruṣarṣabhauc sasainyāḥ prayayuḥ sarve dharmarājābhipūjitāḥa diśaṃ dhanapater iṣṭām ajayat pākaśāsaniḥc bhīmasenas tathā prācīṃ sahadevas tu dakṣiṇāma pratīcīṃ nakulo rājan diśaṃ vyajayad astravitc khāṇḍavaprastham adhyāste dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥd āsīt paramayā lakṣmyā suhṛdgaṇavṛtaḥ prabhuḥ janamejaya uvācaa diśām abhijayaṃ brahman vistareṇānukīrtayac na hi tṛpyāmi pūrveṣāṃ śṛṇvānaś caritaṃ mahat vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa dhanaṃjayasya vakṣyāmi vijayaṃ pūrvam eva tec yaugapadyena pārthair hi vijiteyaṃ vasuṃdharād avāpya rājā rājyārdhaṃ kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥd mahattve rājaśabdasya manaś cakre mahāmanāḥd tadā kṣatraṃ viditvāsya pṛthivīvijayaṃ pratid amarṣāt pārthivendrās te taṃ sameyur yuyutsavaḥd tat sametya bhuvaḥ kṣatraṃ rathanāgāśvapattimatd abhyayāt pārthivaṃ jiṣṇuṃ moghīkartuṃ janādhipad tat pārthaḥ pārthivaṃ kṣatraṃ yuyutsuḥ paramāhaved pratyudyayau mahābāhus tarasā pākaśāsaniḥd tad bhagnaṃ pārthivaṃ kṣatraṃ pārthenākliṣṭakarmaṇād vāyuneva ghanānīkaṃ moghībhūtaṃ yayau diśaḥd taj jitvā pārthivaṃ kṣatraṃ samare paravīrahād yayau tadā vaśe kartum udīcīṃ pāṇḍunandanaḥa pūrvaṃ kuṇindaviṣaye vaśe cakre mahīpatīnc dhanaṃjayo mahābāhur nātitīvreṇa karmaṇād tenaiva sahitaḥ prāyāj jiṣṇuḥ sālvapuraṃ pratid sa sālvapuram āsādya sālvarājaṃ dhanaṃjayaḥd vikrameṇogradhanvānaṃ vaśe cakre mahāmanāḥd taṃ pārthaḥ sahasā jitvā dyumatsenaṃ dhaneśvaramd kṛtvānusainikaṃ prāyāt kaṭadeśam ariṃdamaḥd tatra pāpajitaṃ jiṣṇuḥ sunābhaṃ vasudhādhipamd vikrameṇa vaśe kṛtvā kṛtavān anusainikama ānartān kālakūṭāṃś ca kuṇindāṃś ca vijitya saḥc sumaṇḍalaṃ pāpajitaṃ kṛtavān anusainikama sa tena sahito rājan savyasācī paraṃtapaḥc vijigye sakalaṃ dvīpaṃ prativindhyaṃ ca pārthivama sakaladvīpavāsāṃś ca saptadvīpe ca ye nṛpāḥb tān sarvān ajayat pārtho dharmarājapriyepsayāc arjunasya ca sainyānāṃ vigrahas tumulo bhavata sa tān api maheṣvāso vijitya bharatarṣabhac tair eva sahitaḥ sarvaiḥ prāgjyotiṣam upādravata tatra rājā mahān āsīd bhagadatto viśāṃ patec tenāsīt sumahad yuddhaṃ pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥa sa kirātaiś ca cīnaiś ca vṛtaḥ prāgjyotiṣo bhavatc anyaiś ca bahubhir yodhaiḥ sāgarānūpavāsibhiḥa tataḥ sa divasān aṣṭau yodhayitvā dhanaṃjayamb caturaṅgabalaiḥ sārdhaṃ bhagadattaḥ parājitaḥb pārthasāyakanunnas tu vihvalāṅgo bhṛśāturaḥc prahasann abravīd rājā saṃgrāme vigataklamaḥa upapannaṃ mahābāho tvayi pāṇḍavanandanac pākaśāsanadāyāde vīryam āhavaśobhinia ahaṃ sakhā surendrasya śakrād anavamo raṇec na ca śaknomi te tāta sthātuṃ pramukhato yudhia kim īpsitaṃ pāṇḍaveya brūhi kiṃ karavāṇi tec yad vakṣyasi mahābāho tat kariṣyāmi putraka arjuna uvācaa kurūṇām ṛṣabho rājā dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥb dharmajñaḥ satyasaṃdhaś ca yajvā vipuladakṣiṇaḥc tasya pārthivatām īpse karas tasmai pradīyatāma bhavān pitṛsakhā caiva prīyamāṇo mayāpi cac tato nājñāpayāmi tvāṃ prītipūrvaṃ pradīyatām bhagadatta uvācaa kuntīmātar yathā me tvaṃ tathā rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥb sa tatra satkṛtas tena māsam uṣya dhanaṃjayaḥb udakprācyāṃ vinirjitya prāyād rāmagiriṃ pratib tato rāmagiriṃ jitvā tathā bhuvanaparvatamb anyān api vaśe cakre tarasā pākaśāsaniḥc sarvam etat kariṣyāmi kiṃ cānyat karavāṇi te vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa taṃ vijitya mahābāhuḥ kuntīputro dhanaṃjayaḥc prayayāv uttarāṃ tasmād diśaṃ dhanadapālitāmd evam uktaḥ pratyuvāca bhagadattaṃ dhanaṃjayaḥd anenaiva kṛtaṃ sarvaṃ bhaviṣyaty anujānatāa antargiriṃ ca kaunteyas tathaiva ca bahirgirimc tathoparigiriṃ caiva vijigye puruṣarṣabhaḥa vijitya parvatān sarvān ye ca tatra narādhipāḥc tān vaśe sthāpayitvā sa ratnāny ādāya sarvaśaḥa tair eva sahitaḥ sarvair anurajya ca tān nṛpānc kulūtavāsinaṃ rājan bṛhantam upajagmivāna mṛdaṅgavaranādena rathanemisvanena cac hastināṃ ca ninādena kampayan vasudhām imāma tato bṛhantas taruṇo balena caturaṅgiṇāc niṣkramya nagarāt tasmād yodhayām āsa pāṇḍavama sumahān saṃnipāto bhūd dhanaṃjayabṛhantayoḥc na śaśāka bṛhantas tu soḍhuṃ pāṇḍavavikramama so viṣahyatamaṃ jñātvā kaunteyaṃ parvateśvaraḥc upāvartata durmedhā ratnāny ādāya sarvaśaḥd upacāracchalenāsau pradadau saṃcitān vasūnd arbudaṃ kuñjarāṇāṃ ca nyarbudaṃ vājināṃ tathād tatas tenaiva sahitaḥ kaulūtena dhanaṃjayaḥa sa tad rājyam avasthāpya kulūtasahito yayauc senābindum atho rājan rājyād āśu samākṣipata modāpuraṃ vāmadevaṃ sudāmānaṃ susaṃkulamc kulūtān uttarāṃś caiva tāṃś ca rājñaḥ samānayata tatrasthaḥ puruṣair eva dharmarājasya śāsanātc vyajayad dhanaṃjayo rājan deśān pañca pramāṇataḥa sa divaḥprastham āsādya senābindoḥ puraṃ mahatc balena caturaṅgeṇa niveśam akarot prabhuḥa sa taiḥ parivṛtaḥ sarvair viṣvagaśvaṃ narādhipamc abhyagacchan mahātejāḥ pauravaṃ puruṣarṣabhaḥa vijitya cāhave śūrān pārvatīyān mahārathānc dhvajinyā vyajayad rājan puraṃ pauravarakṣitamd mahatā tatra sainyena pramathyat kurunandanaḥd urasāvalinaṃ caiva romāṇaṃ ca raṇe kṣipata pauravaṃ tu vinirjitya dasyūn parvatavāsinaḥa   senābinduṃ ca tatpurea nyadhāpayad ameyātmāc gaṇān utsavasaṃketān ajayat sapta pāṇḍavaḥa tataḥ kāśmīrakān vīrān kṣatriyān kṣatriyarṣabhaḥc vyajayal lohitaṃ caiva maṇḍalair daśabhiḥ sahaa tatas trigartān kaunteyo dārvān kokanadāś ca yec kṣatriyā bahavo rājann upāvartanta sarvaśaḥa abhisārīṃ tato ramyāṃ vijigye kurunandanaḥc uraśāvāsinaṃ caiva rocamānaṃ raṇe jayata tataḥ siṃhapuraṃ ramyaṃ citrāyudhasurakṣitamc prāmathad balam āsthāya pākaśāsanir āhavea tataḥ suhmāṃś ca colāṃś ca kirīṭī pāṇḍavarṣabhaḥc sahitaḥ sarvasainyena prāmathat kurunandanaḥa tataḥ paramavikrānto bāhlīkān kurunandanaḥc mahatā parimardena vaśe cakre durāsadāna gṛhītvā tu balaṃ sāraṃ phalgu cotsṛjya pāṇḍavaḥc daradān saha kāmbojair ajayat pākaśāsaniḥd yavanāṃś ca mahārāja śakāṃś ca vyajayad yudhid kirātān sabhayān kharvān khalān kācān bahuvṛtānd nīrān utpāsikāṃś caiva mlecchāṃś cānyān sahasraśaḥd tān sarvān ajayat pārtho dharmarājapriyepsayāa prāguttarāṃ diśaṃ ye ca vasanty āśritya dasyavaḥc nivasanti vane ye ca tān sarvān ajayat prabhuḥa lohān paramakāmbojān ṛṣikān uttarān apic sahitāṃs tān mahārāja vyajayat pākaśāsaniḥa ṛṣikeṣu tu saṃgrāmo babhūvātibhayaṃkaraḥc tārakāmayasaṃkāśaḥ paramarṣikapārthayoḥa sa vijitya tato rājann ṛṣikān raṇamūrdhanic śukodarasamaprakhyān hayān aṣṭau samānayate mayūrasadṛśān anyān ubhayān eva cāparānf javanān āśugāṃś caiva karārthaṃ samupānayatf tataḥ sa jitvā bībhatsur bhārataṃ varṣakaṃ tadāf janamejayaḥf anyān vai divyavarṣāṃś ca jitavān kulaparvatānf kathaṃ sa jitavān pārtho divyān varṣān saparvatānf ānupūrvyāc ca me śaṃsa nāmabhiḥ saha vai dvijaf vaiśaṃpāyanaḥf sa jitvā bhārataṃ varṣaṃ balād rājā dhanaṃjayaḥf dasyūṃś cāpy ajayat sarvān kukṣau himavato balāta sa vinirjitya saṃgrāme himavantaṃ saniṣkuṭamc śvetaparvatam āsādya nyavasat puruṣarṣabhaḥ vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa sa śvetaparvataṃ vīraḥ samatikramya bhāratac deśaṃ kiṃpuruṣāvāsaṃ drumaputreṇa rakṣitama mahatā saṃnipātena kṣatriyāntakareṇa hac vyajayat pāṇḍavaśreṣṭhaḥ kare caiva nyaveśayata taṃ jitvā hāṭakaṃ nāma deśaṃ guhyakarakṣitamc pākaśāsanir avyagraḥ sahasainyaḥ samāsadata tāṃs tu sāntvena nirjitya mānasaṃ sara uttamamc ṛṣikulyāś ca tāḥ sarvā dadarśa kurunandanaḥa saro mānasam āsādya hāṭakān abhitaḥ prabhuḥc gandharvarakṣitaṃ deśaṃ vyajayat pāṇḍavas tataḥa tatra tittirikalmāṣān maṇḍūkākṣān hayottamānc lebhe sa karam atyantaṃ gandharvanagarāt tadād hemakūṭam athāsādya nyaviśat phalgunas tadād taṃ hemakūṭaṃ rājendra samatikramya pāṇḍavaḥd harivarṣaṃ viveśātha sainyena mahatā vṛtaḥd tatra pārtho dadarśātha bahūṃś caiva manoramānd nagarāṃś ca vanāṃś caiva nadīś ca vimalodakāḥd puruṣān devakalpāṃś ca nārīś ca priyadarśanāḥd tān sarvāṃs tatra dṛṣṭvātha mudā yukto dhanaṃjayaḥd vaśe cakre ca ratnāni lebhe ca subahūni cad tato niṣadham āsādya giristhān ajayat prabhuḥd atha rājann atikramya niṣadhaṃ śailam āyatamd viveśa madhyamaṃ varṣaṃ pārtho divyam ilāvṛtamd tatra devopamān divyān puruṣān devadarśanānd adṛṣṭapūrvān subhagān sa dadarśa dhanaṃjayaḥd sadanāni ca śubhrāṇi nārīś cāpsarasaṃnibhāḥd dṛṣṭvā tān ajayad ramyān sa taiś ca dadṛśe tadād jitvā ca tān mahābhāgān kare ca viniveśya saḥd ratnāny ādāya divyāni bhūṣaṇair vasanaiḥ sahad udīcīm atha rājendra yayau pārtho mudānvitaḥd sa dadarśa tato meruṃ śikharāṇāṃ prabhuṃ mahatd taṃ kāñcanamayaṃ divyaṃ caturvarṇaṃ durāsadamd āyataṃ śatasāhasraṃ yojanānāṃ tu susthitamd jvalantam acalaṃ meruṃ tejorāśim anuttamamd ākṣipantaṃ prabhāṃ bhānoḥ svaśṛṅgaiḥ kāñcanojjvalaiḥd kāñcanābharaṇaṃ divyaṃ devagandharvasevitamd nityapuṣpaphalopetaṃ siddhacāraṇasevitamd aprameyam anādhṛṣyam adharmabahulair janaiḥd vyālair ācaritaṃ ghorair divyauṣadhividīpitamd svargam āvṛtya tiṣṭhantam ucchrayeṇa mahāgirimd agamyaṃ manasāpy anyair nadīvṛkṣasamanvitamd nānāvihagasaṃghaiś ca nāditaṃ sumanoharaiḥd taṃ dṛṣṭvā phalguno meruṃ prītimān abhavat tadād meror ilāvṛtaṃ varṣaṃ sarvataḥ parimaṇḍalamd meros tu dakṣiṇe pārśve jambūr nāma vanaspatiḥd nityapuṣpaphalopetaḥ siddhacāraṇasevitaḥd āsvargam ucchritā rājaṃs tasya śākhā vanaspateḥd yasya nāmnā tv idaṃ dvīpaṃ jambūdvīpam iti śrutamd tāṃ ca jambūṃ dadarśātha savyasācī paraṃtapaḥd tau dṛṣṭvāpratimau loke jambūṃ meruṃ ca saṃsthitaud prītimān abhavad rājan sarvataḥ sa vilokayand tatra lebhe tato jiṣṇuḥ siddhair divyaiś ca cāraṇaiḥd ratnāni bahusāhasraṃ vastrāṇy ābharaṇāni cad anyāni ca mahārhāṇi tatra labdhvārjunas tadād āmantrayitvā tān sarvān yajñam uddiśya vai guroḥd athādāya bahūn ratnān gamanāyopacakramed meruṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā parvatapravaraṃ prabhuḥd yayau jambūnadītīre nadīṃ śreṣṭhāṃ vilokayand sa tāṃ manoramāṃ divyāṃ jambūsvādurasāvahāmd haimapakṣigaṇair juṣṭāṃ sauvarṇajalajākulāmd haimapaṅkāṃ haimajalāṃ śubhāṃ sauvarṇavālukāmd kva cit sauvarṇapadmaiś ca saṃkulāṃ haimapuṣpakaiḥd kva cit supuṣpitaiḥ kīrṇāṃ suvarṇakumudotpalaiḥd kva cit tīraruhaiḥ kīrṇāṃ haimavṛkṣaiḥ supuṣpitaiḥd tīrthaiś ca rukmasopānaiḥ sarvataḥ saṃkulāṃ śubhāmd vimalair maṇijālaiś ca nṛttagītaravair yutāmd dīptair hemavitānaś ca samantāc chobhitāṃ śubhāmd tathāvidhāṃ nadīṃ dṛṣṭvā pārthas tāṃ praśaśaṃsa had adṛṣṭapūrvāṃ rājendra dṛṣṭvā harṣam avāpa cad darśanīyān nadītīre puruṣān sumanoharānd tān nadīsalilāhārān sadārān amaropamānd nityaṃ sukhamudā yuktān sarvālaṃkāraśobhitānd tebhyo bahūni ratnāni tadā lebhe dhanaṃjayaḥd divyajāmbūnadaṃ haimaṃ bhūṣaṇāni ca peśalamd labdhvā tān durlabhān pārthaḥ pratīcīṃ prayayau diśamd nāgānāṃ rakṣitaṃ deśam ajayac cārjunas tataḥd tato gatvā mahārāja vāruṇīṃ pākaśāsaniḥd gandhamādanam āsādya tatrasthān ajayat prabhuḥd taṃ gandhamādanaṃ rājann atikramya tato rjunaḥd ketumālaṃ viveśātha varṣaṃ ratnasamanvitamd sevitaṃ devakalpaiś ca nārībhiḥ priyadarśanaiḥd taṃ jitvā cārjuno rājan kare ca viniveśya cad āhṛtya tatra ratnāni durlabhāni tathārjunaḥd punaś ca parivṛtyātha madhyaṃ deśam ilāvṛtamd gatvā prācīṃ diśaṃ rājan savyasācī paraṃtapaḥd merumandarayor madhye śailodām abhito nadīmd ye te kīcakaveṇūnāṃ chāyāṃ ramyām upāsated khaṣāñ jhaṣāṃś ca nadyotān praghasān dīrghaveṇikānd paśupāṃś ca kuṇindāṃś ca ṭaṅkaṇān paraṭaṅkaṇānd etān samastāñ jitvā ca kare ca viniveśya cad ratnāny ādāya sarvebhyo mālyavantaṃ tato yayaud taṃ mālyavantaṃ śailendraṃ samatikramya pāṇḍavaḥd bhadrāśvaṃ praviveśātha varṣaṃ svargopamaṃ śubhamd tatrāmaropamān ramyān puruṣān sukhasaṃyutānd jitvā tān svavaśe kṛtvā kare ca viniveśya cad āhṛtya sarvaratnāni asaṃkhyāni tatas tataḥd nīlaṃ nāma giriṃ gatvā tatrasthān ajayat prabhuḥd tato jiṣṇur atikramya parvataṃ nīlam āyatamd viveśa ramyakaṃ varṣaṃ saṃkīrṇaṃ mithunaiḥ śubhaiḥd taṃ deśam atha jitvā sa kare ca viniveśya cad ajayac cāpi bībhatsur deśaṃ guhyakarakṣitamd tatra lebhe ca rājendra sauvarṇān mṛgapakṣiṇaḥd agṛhṇad yajñabhūtyarthaṃ ramaṇīyān manoramānd anyāni labdhvā ratnāni pāṇḍavo tha mahābalaḥd gandharvarakṣitaṃ deśam ajayat sagaṇaṃ tadād tatra ratnāni divyāni labdhvā rājann athārjunaḥd śvetaparvatam āsādya jitvā parvatavāsinaḥd sa śvetaṃ parvataṃ rājan samatikramya pāṇḍavaḥd varṣaṃ hiraṇyakaṃ nāma viveśātha mahīpated sa tu deśeṣu ramyeṣu gantuṃ tatropacakramed madhye prāsādavṛndeṣu nakṣatrāṇāṃ śaśī yathād mahāpatheṣu rājendra sarvato yāntam arjunamd prāsādavaraśṛṅgasthāḥ parayā vīryaśobhayād dadṛśus tāḥ striyaḥ sarvāḥ pārtham ātmayaśaskaramd taṃ kalāpadharaṃ śūraṃ sarathaṃ sānugaṃ prabhumd savarmaṃ sakirīṭaṃ vai saṃnaddhaṃ saparicchadamd sukumāraṃ mahāsattvaṃ tejorāśim anuttamamd śakropamam amitraghnaṃ paravāraṇavāraṇamd paśyantaḥ strīgaṇās tatra śaktipāṇiṃ sma menired ayaṃ sa puruṣavyāghro raṇe dbhutaparākramaḥd asya bāhubalaṃ prāpya na bhavanty asuhṛdgaṇāḥd iti vāco bruvantyas tāḥ striyaḥ premṇā dhanaṃjayamd tuṣṭuvuḥ puṣpavṛṣṭiṃ ca sasṛjus tasya mūrdhanid dṛṣṭvā te tu mudā yuktāḥ kautūhalasamanvitāḥd ratnair vibhūṣaṇaiś caiva abhyavarṣanta pāṇḍavamd atha jitvā samastāṃs tān kare ca viniveśya cad maṇihemapravālāni vastrāṇy ābharaṇāni cad vaiśaṃpāyanaḥd etāni labdhvā pārtho pi śṛṅgavantaṃ giriṃ yayaud śṛṅgavantaṃ ca kaunteyaḥ samatikramya phalgunaḥa uttaraṃ harivarṣaṃ tu samāsādya sa pāṇḍavaḥb vidyādharagaṇāṃś caiva yakṣendrāṃś ca vinirjayanb tatra lebhe mahātmā vai vāso divyam anuttamamb kiṃnaradrumapatrāṃś ca tatra kṛṣṇājinān bahūnb yājñīyāṃs tāṃs tadā divyāṃs tatra lebhe dhanaṃjayaḥc iyeṣa jetuṃ taṃ deśaṃ pākaśāsananandanaḥa tata enaṃ mahākāyā mahāvīryā bharatarṣabhaḥc saṃgrāmān subahūn kṛtvā kṣatriyair dasyubhis tathāa sa vinirjitya rājñas tān kare ca viniveśya hac dhanāny ādāya sarvebhyo ratnāni vividhāni caa hayāṃs tittirikalmāṣāñ śukapatranibhān apic mayūrasadṛśāṃś cānyān sarvān anilaraṃhasaḥa vṛtaḥ sumahatā rājan balena caturaṅgiṇāc ājagāma punar vīraḥ śakraprasthaṃ purottamamd dharmarājāya tat pārtho dhanaṃ sarvaṃ savāhanamd nyavedayad anujñātas tena rājñā gṛhān yayau vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa etasminn eva kāle tu bhīmaseno pi vīryavānc dharmarājam anujñāpya yayau prācīṃ diśaṃ pratia mahatā balacakreṇa pararāṣṭrāvamardināb yuddhaṃ nirāyudhama bhīmasenas tu tad dṛṣṭvā tasya karma paraṃtapaḥb balaṃ sarvam avaṣṭabhya paricakrāma maṇḍalamb pothayitvā puraṃ sarvaṃ suvarmāṇaṃ tato jayatc adhisenāpatiṃ cakre sudharmāṇaṃ mahābalama tataḥ prācīṃ diśaṃ bhīmo yayau bhīmaparākramaḥc sainyena mahatā rājan kampayann iva medinīma so śvamedheśvaraṃ rājan rocamānaṃ sahānujamc jigāya samare vīro balena balināṃ varaḥa sa taṃ pauṇḍrādhipaṃ vīraṃ vāsudevaṃ mahābalamb idānīṃ vṛṣṇivīryeṇa na yotsyāmīti pauṇḍrakaḥb kṛṣṇasya bhujasaṃtrāsāt karam āśu dadau nṛpaḥc kauśikīkacchanilayaṃ rājānaṃ ca mahaujasama ubhau balavṛtau vīrāv yayauc tatra nīlena rājñā sa cakre yuddhaṃ nararṣabhaḥa pāṇḍavaḥ paravīraghnaḥ sahadevaḥ pratāpavānc tato sya sumahad yuddham āsīd bhīrubhayaṃkarama sainyakṣayakaraṃ caiva prāṇānāṃ saṃśayāya cac cakre sviṣṭakṛttamaḥc abhayaṃ ca sa jagrāha svasainye vai mahīpatiḥa tataḥ prabhṛti ye ke cid ajñānāt tāṃ purīṃ nṛpāḥc jigīṣanti balād rājaṃs te dahyantīha vahnināa tasyāṃ puryāṃ tadā caiva māhiṣmatyāṃ citrabhānuḥ sureśaś ca analas tvaṃ vibhāvasuḥb agnir duḥsparśanaś cāsi hutāśo jvalanaḥ śikhīb vaiśvānaras tvaṃ piṅgeśa bhūritejāḥ plavaṃgamaḥb kumārasūnur bhagavān rukmagarbho hiraṇyakṛtb citrabhānuḥ sureśaś ca analas tvaṃ vibhāvasob svargadvāraspṛśaś cāsi hutāśo jvalanaḥ śikhīb vaiśvānaras tvaṃ piṅgeśaḥ plavaṃgo bhūritejasaḥb kumārasūs tvaṃ bhagavān rudradharmo hiraṇyakṛtb agnir dadātu me tejo vāyuḥ prāṇaṃ dadātu meb pṛthivī balam ādadhyāc chivaṃ cāpo diśantu meb apāṃ garbha mahāsattva jātavedaḥ sureśvarab devānāṃ mukham agne tvaṃ satyena vipunīhi māmb ṛṣibhir brāhmaṇaiś caiva daivatair asurair apib nityaṃ suhuta yajñeṣu satyena vipunīhi māmb dhūmaketuḥ śikhī ca tvaṃ pāpahānilasaṃbhavaḥb sarvaprāṇiṣu nityasthaḥ satyena vipunīhi māmb evaṃ stuto si bhagavan prītena śucinā mayāb vaiśaṃpāyana uvācab tuṣṭiṃ puṣṭiṃ smṛtiṃ caiva prītiṃ cāgne prayaccha meb ity evaṃ mantram āgneyaṃ paṭhan yo juhuyād vibhumb ṛddhimān satataṃ dāntaḥ sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyatec yajñavighnam imaṃ kartuṃ nārhas tvaṃ havyavāhanaa evam uktvā tu mādreyaḥ kuśair āstīrya medinīmc vidhivat puruṣavyāghraḥ pāvakaṃ pratyupāviśata pramukhe sarvasainyasya bhītodvignasya bhāratac na cainam atyagād vahnir velām iva mahodadhiḥa tam abhyetya śanair vahnir uvāca kurunandanamc sahadevaṃ nṛṇāṃ devaṃ sāntvapūrvam idaṃ vacaḥa uttiṣṭhottiṣṭha kauravya jijñāseyaṃ kṛtā mayāb devadevasya kṛṣṇasya viṣṇor amitatejasaḥb bhujam āśritya yajñaṃ taṃ cikīrṣuṃ pāṇḍunandanamb jānāmi sahadevādya kṛtārtho yāhi sāṃpratamc vedmi sarvam abhiprāyaṃ tava dharmasutasya caa mayā tu rakṣitavyeyaṃ purī bharatasattamac yāvad rājño sya nīlasya kulavaṃśadharā itie īpsitaṃ tu kariṣyāmi manasas tava pāṇḍavaa tata utthāya hṛṣṭātmā prāñjaliḥ śirasānataḥc pūjayām āsa mādreyaḥ pāvakaṃ puruṣarṣabhaḥa pāvake vinivṛtte tu nīlo rājābhyayāt tadāb pāvakasyājñayā cainam arcayām āsa pārthivaḥc satkāreṇa naravyāghraṃ sahadevaṃ yudhāṃ patima pratigṛhya ca tāṃ pūjāṃ kare ca viniveśya tamc mādrīsutas tataḥ prāyād vijayī dakṣiṇāṃ diśama traipuraṃ sa vaśe kṛtvā rājānam amitaujasamc nijagrāha mahābāhus tarasā potaneśvarama āhṛtiṃ kauśikācāryaṃ yatnena mahatā tataḥc vaśe cakre mahābāhuḥ surāṣṭrādhipatiṃ tathāa surāṣṭraviṣayasthaś ca preṣayām āsa rukmiṇec rājñe bhojakaṭasthāya mahāmātrāya dhīmatea bhīṣmakāya sa dharmātmā sākṣād indrasakhāya vaic sa cāsya sasuto rājan pratijagrāha śāsanama prītipūrvaṃ mahābāhur vāsudevam avekṣya cac tataḥ sa ratnāny ādāya punaḥ prāyād yudhāṃ patiḥa tataḥ śūrpārakaṃ caiva gaṇaṃ copakṛtāhvayamc vaśe cakre mahātejā daṇḍakāṃś ca mahābalaḥa sāgaradvīpavāsāṃś ca nṛpatīn mlecchayonijānc niṣādān puruṣādāṃś ca karṇaprāvaraṇān apid niṣādān ajayat tatra sāgaramlecchayonijāna ye ca kālamukhā nāma narā rākṣasayonayaḥb ye caikapādā manujā vṛkṣakoṭaraśāyinaḥc kṛtsnaṃ kollagiriṃ caiva muracīpattanaṃ tathāa dvīpaṃ tāmrāhvayaṃ caiva parvataṃ rāmakaṃ tathāc timiṃgilaṃ ca nṛpatiṃ vaśe cakre mahāmatiḥa ekapādāṃś ca puruṣān kevalān vanavāsinaḥc nagarīṃ saṃjayantīṃ ca picchaṇḍaṃ karahāṭakame dūtair eva vaśe cakre karaṃ cainān adāpayatf bhṛgukacchaṃ gato dhīmān daṇḍenāmitrakarśanaḥf barbarān pāraśān anyān dvīpavāsān vaśe vaśīf tūlakān daradāṃś cānyān sindhurān vanavāsinaḥf aśmakān mūlakāṃś caiva vidarbhāṃś ca mahābalānf dūtair eva vaśe cakre kare ca viniveśya saḥf tataḥ kusṛtivītajñān dakṣiṇāpathavāsinaḥf ajayat saṃyuge tatra dharmamārgeṇa pāṇḍavaḥa pāṇḍyāṃś ca draviḍāṃś caiva sahitāṃś coḍrakeralaiḥb siṃhaladvīpakān anyān dūtaiś cakre vaśe balātb ghaṭotkacaṃ mahābāhuṃ rākṣasaṃ ghoradarśanamb āgamyatām iti prāha dharmarājasya śāsanātb sarvasvaṃ karam ādāya tair eva sahito nṛpaḥb uttaraṃ tīram āsādya sāgarasyormimālinaḥb sa rākṣasaparīvāras taṃ praṇamyāśu saṃsthitaḥc andhrāṃs talavanāṃś caiva kaliṅgān oṣṭrakarṇikāna antākhīṃ caiva romāṃ ca yavanānāṃ puraṃ tathāc dūtair eva vaśe cakre karaṃ cainān adāpayatd kānanadvīpakāṃś caiva tarasātītya cāhaved tāmraparṇīṃ tato gatvā kanyātīrtham atītya cad dakṣiṇāṃ ca diśaṃ sarvāṃ vijitya kurunandanad sahadevas tato rājan mantribhiḥ saha tatra vaid saṃpradhārya mahābāhuḥ sacivair buddhimattaraiḥd cintayām āsa kauravyo bhrātṛputraṃ ghaṭotkacamd tataś cintitamātras tu rākṣasaḥ pratyadṛśyatad atidīrgho mahābāhuḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaḥd abhivādya tato rājan sahadevaṃ ghaṭotkacaḥd prahvaḥ kṛtāñjalis tasthau kiṃ kāryam iti cābravītd taṃ meruśikharākāram āgataṃ pāṇḍunandanaḥa bharukacchaṃ gato dhīmān dūtān mādravatīsutaḥc preṣayām āsa rājendra paulastyāya mahātmanee vibhīṣaṇāya dharmātmā prītipūrvam ariṃdamaḥa sa cāsya pratijagrāha śāsanaṃ prītipūrvakamc tac ca kālakṛtaṃ dhīmān anvamanyata sa prabhuḥd bibhīṣaṇo mahātman yad īpsitaṃ karavāṇy ahama tataḥ saṃpreṣayām āsa ratnāni vividhāni cac candanāgurumukhyāni divyāny ābharaṇāni caa vāsāṃsi ca mahārhāṇi maṇīṃś caiva mahādhanānb prītimān abhavad dṛṣṭvā ratnaughaṃ taṃ ca pāṇḍavaḥb janamejayaḥb icchāmy āgamanaṃ śrotuṃ haiḍimbasya dvijottamab laṅkāyāṃ ca gatiṃ brahman paulastyasya ca darśanamb kāverīdarśanaṃ caiva rājānaḥ sarva eva tānb ānupūrvyāc ca me śaṃsa sarvaṃ brāhmaṇapuṃgavab vaiśaṃpāyanaḥb śṛṇu rājan purā vṛttaṃ sahadevasya sāhasamb kānanadvīpakāṃś caiva tarasā jitya cāhaveb dakṣiṇāṃ ca diśaṃ jitvā colasya viṣayaṃ yayaub dadarśa puṇyatoyāṃ vai kāverīṃ saritāṃ varāmb nānāpakṣigaṇair juṣṭāṃ tāpasair upaśobhitāmb sālalodhrārjunair bilvair jambūśalmalikiṃśukaiḥb kadambaiḥ saptaparṇaiś ca kāśmaryāmalakair vṛtāmb nyagrodhaiś ca mahāśākhaiḥ plakṣair audumbarair apib śamīpalāśavṛkṣaiś ca aśvatthaiḥ khadirair vṛtāmb badarībhiś ca saṃpannām aśvakarṇaiś ca śobhitāmb karañjatintriṇīkaiś ca tālavrātair alaṃkṛtāmb śirīṣaiḥ kuṭajair nimbair madhūkaiḥ kṣīrakair vṛtāmb puṃnāgair bakulaiḥ kundaiś campakaiḥ sarvato vṛtāmb priyaṅgvaśokatilakair atimuktaiś ca śobhitāmb asanaiḥ karṇikāraiś ca nāgavṛkṣair alaṃkṛtāmb ketakībhiḥ kurabakair jātiyūthikakundalaiḥb aṅkolaiḥ karavīraiś ca puṃnāgaiḥ pāṭalair vṛtāmb kramukair nālikeraiś ca panasāmraiś ca śobhitāmb cūtaiḥ puṇḍrakapatraiś ca kadalyāḍhakasaṃvṛtāmb nīpaiś ca vetasaiḥ kīrṇāṃ nālakundakuśair vṛtāmb evaṃ bahuvidhair vṛkṣair divyair anyaiś ca śobhitāmb haṃsakāraṇḍavaiḥ kīrṇāṃ kuraraiḥ sārasaiḥ śukaiḥb cakravākagaṇair juṣṭāṃ plavaiś ca jalavāyasaiḥb samudrakākaiḥ krauñcaiś ca nāditāṃ jalakukkuṭaiḥb evaṃ khagaiś ca bahubhiḥ saṃghuṣṭāṃ jalacāribhiḥb āśramair bahubhir yuktāṃ caityavṛkṣaiś ca śobhitāmb sevitāṃ brāhmaṇaiḥ śubhrair vedavedāṅgapāragaiḥb kva cit tīraruhair vṛkṣair mālābhir iva śobhitāmb puṣpagulmalatopetām aṅganām iva bhūṣaṇaiḥb kva cit patracitaiḥ padmaiḥ kva cit saugandhikotpalaiḥb kahlārakumudaiḥ phullaiḥ kamalair upaśobhitāmb nānāpuṣparajodhvastāṃ pramadām iva bhūṣitāmb ramaṇīyāṃ tathā hṛdyāṃ vihṛtām apsarogaṇaiḥb mṛṣṭatīrthām akaluṣāṃ prāṇināṃ jīvanīṃ śubhāmb apārāṃ svādutoyāṃ vai pulinadvīpaśobhitāmb kāverīṃ tādṛśīṃ dṛṣṭvā prītimān pāṇḍavo bravītb asmadrāṣṭre yathā gaṅgā kāverī ca tathā ihab sahadevas tu tāṃ tīrtvā nadīm anucaraiḥ sahab dakṣiṇaṃ tīram āsādya gamanāyopacakrameb āgataṃ pāṇḍavaṃ tatra śrutvā viṣayavāsinaḥb darśanārthaṃ yayus te tu kautūhalasamanvitāḥb dramiḷāḥ puruṣā rājan striyaś ca priyadarśanāḥb gatvā pāṇḍusutaṃ tatra dadṛśus te mudānvitāḥb sukumāraṃ viśālākṣaṃ vrajantaṃ tridaśopamamb darśanīyatamaṃ loke netrair animiṣair ivab āścaryabhūtaṃ dadṛśur dramiḷās te samāhitāḥb mahāsenopamaṃ dṛṣṭvā pūjāṃ cakruś ca tasya vaib ratnaiś ca vividhair iṣṭair bhogair anyaiś ca saṃmataiḥb gītamaṅgalayuktābhiḥ stuvanto nakulānujamb sahadevas tu tān dṛṣṭvā dramilān āgatāṃs tadāb visṛjya tān mahārāja prasthito dakṣiṇāṃ diśamb dūtena tarasā colaṃ vijitya dramiḷeśvaramb tato ratnāny upādāya pāṇḍyasya viṣayaṃ yayaub darśane sahadevasya na ca tṛptā narāḥ pareb gacchantam anugacchantaḥ prītyā kautūhalānvitāḥb tato mādrīsuto rājan mṛgavrātān vyalokayatb gajān vanacarān anyān vyāghrān kṛṣṇamṛgān bahūnb śukān mayūrān dṛṣṭvā tu gṛdhrān āraṇyakukkuṭānb tato deśaṃ samāsādya śvaśurasya mahīpateḥb preṣayām āsa mādreyo dūtān pāṇḍyāya vai tadāb pratijagrāha tasyājñāṃ saṃprītyā malayadhvajaḥb bhāryā rūpavatī jiṣṇoḥ pāṇḍyasya tanayā śubhāb citrāṅgadeti vikhyātā dramilā yoṣitāṃ varāb āgataṃ sahadevaṃ tu sā śrutvāntaḥpure pituḥb preṣayām āsa saṃprītyā pūjāṃ ratnāni vai bahub pāṇḍyo pi bahuratnāni dūtaiḥ saha mumoca hab maṇimuktāpravālāṃś ca śaṅkhaśuktiyutān bahūnb tāṃ dṛṣṭvā prītimān pūjāṃ pāṇḍavo tha mudā nṛpab bhrātuḥ putre bahūn ratnān adadād babhruvāhaneb pāṇḍyaṃ dramiḷarājānaṃ śvaśuraṃ malayadhvajamb sa dūtais taṃ vaśe kṛtvā maṇalūreśvaraṃ tadāb tato ratnāny upādāya dramiḷair āvṛto yayaub agastyasyālayaṃ divyaṃ devalokasamaṃ girimb sa taṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā malayaṃ bharatarṣabhab laṅghayitvā tu mādreyas tāmraparṇīṃ nadīṃ śubhāmb prasannasalilāṃ divyāṃ suśītāṃ candanodvahāmb samudratīram āsādya nyaviśat pāṇḍunandanaḥb vaiśaṃpāyanaḥb sahadevas tato rājan mantribhiḥ saha bhāratab saṃpradhārya mahābāhuḥ sacivair buddhimattaraiḥb anumānya sa tāṃ rājan sahadevas tvarānvitaḥb cintayām āsa rājendra bhrātuḥ putraṃ ghaṭotkacamb tataś cintitamātre tu rākṣasaḥ pratyadṛśyatab atidīrgho mahākāyaḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaḥb nīlajīmūtasaṃkāśas taptakāñcanakuṇḍalaḥb vicitrahārakeyūraḥ kiṅkiṇīmaṇibhūṣitaḥb hemamālī mahādaṃṣṭraḥ kirīṭī kukṣibandhanaḥb tāmrakeśo hariśmaśrur bhīmākṣaḥ kanakāṅgadaḥb raktacandanadigdhāṅgaḥ sūkṣmāmbaradharo balīb javena sa yayau tatra cālayann iva medinīmb tato dṛṣṭvā janā rājann āyāntaṃ parvatopamamb bhayād dhi dudruvuḥ sarve siṃhāt kṣudramṛgā yathāb āsasāda ca mādreyaṃ pulastyaṃ rāvaṇo yathāb abhivādya tato rājan sahadevaṃ ghaṭotkacaḥb prahvaḥ kṛtāñjalis tasthau kiṃ kāryam iti cābravītb taṃ meruśikharākāram āgataṃ pāṇḍunandanaḥb taṃ pariṣvajya bāhubhyāṃ mūrdhny upāghrāya cāsakṛtb sahadevaḥb pūjayitvā sahāmātyaḥ prīto vākyam uvāca hab gaccha laṅkāṃ purīṃ vatsa karārthaṃ mama śāsanātb tatra dṛṣṭvā mahātmānaṃ rākṣasendraṃ vibhīṣaṇamb ratnāni rājasūyārthaṃ vividhāni bahūni cab vaiśaṃpāyanaḥb upādāya ca sarvāṇi pratyāgaccha mahābalab pāṇḍavenaivam uktas tu mudā yukto ghaṭotkacaḥb tathety uktvā mahārāja pratasthe dakṣiṇāṃ diśamb yayau pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā sahadevaṃ ghaṭotkacaḥb laṅkām abhimukho rājan samudram avalokayatb kūrmagrāhajhaṣākīrṇaṃ mīnair nakrais tathākulamb śuktivrātaiḥ samākīrṇaṃ śaṅkhānāṃ nicayākulamb sa dṛṣṭvā rāmasetuṃ ca cintayan rāmavikramamb praṇamya tam atikramya yāmyāṃ velām alokayatb gatvā pāraṃ samudrasya dakṣiṇaṃ sa ghaṭotkacaḥb dadarśa laṅkāṃ rājendra nākapṛṣṭhopamāṃ śubhāmb prākāreṇāvṛtāṃ ramyāṃ śubhadvāraiś ca śobhitāmb prāsādair bahusāhasraiḥ śvetaraktaiś ca saṃkulāmb tāpanīyagavākṣeṇa muktājālāntarāṇi cab haimarājatajālena dāntajālaiś ca śobhitāmb harmyagopurasaṃbādhāṃ rukmatoraṇasaṃkulāmb divyadundubhinirhrādām udyānavanaśobhitāmb sarvakālaphalair vṛkṣaiḥ puṣpitair upaśobhitāmb puṣpagandhaiś ca saṃkīrṇāṃ ramaṇīyamahāpathāmb nānāratnaiś ca saṃpūrṇām indrasyevāmarāvatīmb viveśa sa purīṃ laṅkāṃ rākṣasaiś ca niṣevitāmb dadarśa rākṣasavrātāñ śūlaprāsadharān bahūnb nānāveṣadharān dakṣān nārīś ca priyadarśanāḥb divyamālyāmbaradharā divyabhūṣaṇabhūṣitāḥb madaraktāntanayanāḥ pīnaśroṇipayodharāḥb bhaimaseniṃ tato dṛṣṭvā hṛṣṭās te vismayaṃ gatāḥb āsasāda gṛhaṃ rājña indrasya sadanopamamb ghaṭotkacaḥb sa dvārapālam āsādya vākyam etad uvāca hab kurūṇām ṛṣabho rājā pāṇḍur nāma mahābalaḥb kanīyāṃs tasya dāyādaḥ sahadeva iti śrutaḥb kṛṣṇamitrasya tu guro rājasūyārtham udyataḥb tenāhaṃ preṣito dūtaḥ karārthaṃ kauravasya cab draṣṭum icchāmi rājendraṃ tvaṃ kṣipraṃ māṃ nivedayab vaiśaṃpāyanaḥb tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā dvārapālo mahīpateḥb tathety uktvā viveśātha bhavanaṃ sa nivedakaḥb sāñjaliḥ sa samācaṣṭa sarvāṃ dūtagiraṃ tadāb dvārapālavacaḥ śrutvā rākṣasendro vibhīṣaṇaḥb uvāca vākyaṃ dharmātmā samīpaṃ me praveśyatāmb evam uktas tu rājendra dharmajñena mahātmanāb atha niṣkramya saṃbhrānto dvāḥstho haiḍimbam abravītb ehi dūta nṛpaṃ draṣṭuṃ kṣipraṃ praviśa ca svayamb dvārapālavacaḥ śrutvā praviveśa ghaṭotkacaḥb sa praviśya dadarśātha rākṣasendrasya mandiramb tataḥ kailāsasaṃkāśaṃ taptakāñcanatoraṇamb prākāreṇa parikṣiptaṃ gopuraiś cāpi śobhitamb harmyaprāsādasaṃbādhaṃ nānāratnasamanvitamb kāñcanais tāpanīyaiś ca sphāṭikai rājatair apib vajravaiḍūryagarbhaiś ca stambhair dṛṣṭimanoharaiḥb nānādhvajapatākābhir yuktaṃ maṇivicitritamb citramālyāvṛtaṃ ramyaṃ taptakāñcanavedikamb tān dṛṣṭvā tatra sarvān sa bhaimasenir manoramānb praviśann eva haiḍimbaḥ śuśrāva muravasvanamb tantrīgītasamākīrṇaṃ samatālamitākṣaramb divyadundubhinirhrādaṃ vāditraśatasaṃkulamb sa śrutvā madhuraṃ śabdaṃ prītimān abhavat tadāb tato vigāhya haiḍimbo bahukakṣyāṃ manoramāmb sa dadarśa mahātmānaṃ dvāḥsthena saha bhāratab taṃ vibhīṣaṇam āsīnaṃ kāñcane paramāsaneb divye bhāskarasaṃkāśe muktāmaṇivibhūṣiteb divyābharaṇacitrāṅgaṃ divyarūpadharaṃ vibhumb divyamālyāmbaradharaṃ divyagandhokṣitaṃ śubhamb vibhrājamānaṃ vapuṣā sūryavaiśvānaraprabhamb upopaviṣṭaṃ sacivair devair iva śatakratumb yakṣair mahārathair divyair nārībhiḥ priyadarśanaiḥb gīrbhir maṅgalayuktābhiḥ pūjyamānaṃ yathāvidhib cāmare vyajane cāgrye hemadaṇḍe mahādhaneb gṛhīte varanārībhyāṃ dhūyamāne ca mūrdhanib arciṣmantaṃ śriyā juṣṭaṃ kuberavaruṇopamamb dharme caiva sthitaṃ nityam adbhutaṃ rākṣaseśvaramb dṛṣṭvā ghaṭotkaco rājan vavande taṃ kṛtāñjaliḥb prahvas tasthau mahāvīryaḥ śakraṃ citraratho yathāb taṃ dūtam āgataṃ dṛṣṭvā rākṣasendro vibhīṣaṇaḥb vibhīṣaṇaḥb pūjayitvā yathānyāyaṃ sāntvapūrvaṃ vaco bravītb kasya vaṃśe nu saṃjātaḥ pitāmaha vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa tato bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo buddhyā niścitya bhāratac vārṣṇeyaṃ manyate kṛṣṇam arhaṇīyatamaṃ bhuvia eṣa hy eṣāṃ sametānāṃ tejobalaparākramaiḥc madhye tapann ivābhāti jyotiṣām iva bhāskaraḥa asūryam iva sūryeṇa nivātam iva vāyunāc bhāsitaṃ hlāditaṃ caiva kṛṣṇenedaṃ sado hi naḥa tasmai bhīṣmābhyanujñātaḥ sahadevaḥ pratāpavānc upajahre tha vidhivad vārṣṇeyāyārghyam uttamamd gām arghyaṃ madhuparkaṃ cāpy ānīyāpāharat tadād caraṇāv aspṛśac chaureḥ sahadevo viśāṃ pated keśavaś cāpy upāghrāya mūrdhni śastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥd sahadevam athovāca kaccid vaḥ kuśalaṃ gṛhed so pi taṃ tu tathety āha sarvaṃ nanu tavājñayād etasminn antare rājann idam āsīd athādbhutamd tāṃ dṛṣṭvā kṣatriyāḥ sarve pūjāṃ kṛṣṇasya bhūyasīmd saṃprekṣyānyonyam āsīnā hṛdayais tām adhārayana pratijagrāha tat kṛṣṇaḥ śāstradṛṣṭena karmaṇāc śiśupālas tu tāṃ pūjāṃ vāsudeve na cakṣamea sa upālabhya bhīṣmaṃ ca dharmarājaṃ ca saṃsadic apākṣipad vāsudevaṃ cedirājo mahābalaḥd teṣām ākārabhāvajñaḥ sahadevo na cakṣamed mānināṃ balināṃ rājñāṃ puraḥ saṃdarśite paded puṣpavṛṣṭir mahaty āsīt sahadevasya mūrdhanid janmaprabhṛti vṛṣṇīnāṃ sunīthaḥ śatrur abravītd praṣṭā viyonijo rājā prativaktā nadīsutaḥd pratigrahītā gopālaḥ pradātā ca viyonijaḥd sadasyā mūkavat sarve āsate tra kim ucyated ity uktvā sa vihasyāśu pāṇḍavaṃ punar abravītd atipaśyasi vā sarvān na vā paśyasi pāṇḍavad tiṣṭhatsv anyeṣu pūjyeṣu gopam arcitavān asid ete caivobhaye tāta kāryasya tu vināśaked atidṛṣṭir adṛṣṭir vā tayoḥ kiṃ tvaṃ samāsthitaḥ śiśupāla uvācaa nāyam arhati vārṣṇeyas tiṣṭhatsv iha mahātmasuc mahīpatiṣu kauravya rājavat pārthivārhaṇama nāyaṃ yuktaḥ samācāraḥ pāṇḍaveṣu mahātmasuc yat kāmāt puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ pāṇḍavārcitavān asia bālā yūyaṃ na jānīdhvaṃ dharmaḥ sūkṣmo hi pāṇḍavāḥc ayaṃ tatrābhyatikrānta āpageyo lpadarśanaḥa tvādṛśo dharmayukto hi kurvāṇaḥ priyakāmyayāc bhavaty abhyadhikaṃ bhīṣmo lokeṣv avamataḥ satāma kathaṃ hy arājā dāśārho madhye sarvamahīkṣitāmc arhaṇām arhati tathā yathā yuṣmābhir arcitaḥa atha vā manyase kṛṣṇaṃ sthaviraṃ bharatarṣabhac vasudeve sthite vṛddhe katham arhati tatsutaḥa atha vā vāsudevo pi priyakāmo nuvṛttavānc drupade tiṣṭhati kathaṃ mādhavo rhati pūjanama ācāryaṃ manyase kṛṣṇam atha vā kurupuṃgavac droṇe tiṣṭhati vārṣṇeyaṃ kasmād arcitavān asia ṛtvijaṃ manyase kṛṣṇam atha vā kurunandanac dvaipāyane sthite vipre kathaṃ kṛṣṇo rcitas tvayād bhīṣme śāṃtanave rājan sthite puruṣasattamed svacchandamṛtyuke rājan kathaṃ kṛṣṇo rcitas tvayād aśvatthāmni sthite vīre sarvaśāstraviśāraded kathaṃ kṛṣṇas tvayā rājann arcitaḥ kurunandanad duryodhane ca rājendre sthite puruṣasattamed kṛpe ca bhāratācārye kathaṃ kṛṣṇas tvayārcitaḥd drumaṃ kiṃpuruṣācāryam atikramya tathārcitaḥd bhīṣmake ca durādharṣe pāṇḍye ca kṛtalakṣaṇed nṛpe ca rukmiṇi śreṣṭhe ekalavye tathaiva cad śalye madrādhipe caiva kathaṃ kṛṣṇo rcitas tvayād ayaṃ ca sarvarājñāṃ yo balaślāghī mahārathaḥd jāmadagnyasya dayitaḥ śiṣyo viprasya bhāratad yenātmabalam āśritya rājāno yudhi nirjitāḥd taṃ ca karṇam atikramya kathaṃ kṛṣṇo rcitas tvayād bhīṣme śāṃtanave rājan sthite puruṣasattamed svacchandamṛtyuke tasmin kathaṃ kṛṣṇo rcitas tvayād kṛpe ca bhāratācārye kathaṃ kṛṣṇo rcitas tvayād aśvatthāmni sthite vīre sarvaśastraviśāraded kathaṃ kṛṣṇas tvayā rājann arcito yadunandanaḥd drume kiṃpuruṣācārye kathaṃ kṛṣṇas tvayārcitaḥd ayaṃ pārthād anavamo dhanurvede parākramed ekalavye sthite rājan kathaṃ kṛṣṇas tvayārcitaḥd bhagadatte mahāvīrye jayatsene ca māgadhed kāliṅge ca sthite rājan kathaṃ kṛṣṇas tvayārcitaḥd pūrvadeśādhipe vīre kausalendre bṛhadbaled virāṭe ca sthite vīre kathaṃ kṛṣṇo rcitas tvayād bhīṣmake ca durādharṣe pāṇḍye ca kṛtadhanvanid nṛpe rukmiṇi ca śreṣṭhe dantavakre ca pārthived śalye madrādhipe caiva kathaṃ kṛṣṇas tvayārcitaḥd surāṣṭrādhipatau vīre mālave ca sthite nṛped kṛtakṣaṇe ca vaidehe kathaṃ kṛṣṇas tvayārcitaḥd ayaṃ ca sarvarājñāṃ yo balaślāghī mahārathaḥd jāmadagnyasya dayitaḥ śiṣyo viprasya bhāratad yenātmabalam āśritya jarāsaṃdho yudhā jitaḥd taṃ karṇaṃ samatikramya kathaṃ kṛṣṇas tvayārcitaḥd vindānuvindāv āvantyau kāmbhojaṃ ca sudakṣiṇamd sthite sālve ca rājendre kathaṃ kṛṣṇo rcitas tvayād asmin pārthasakhe rājan gandharvāṇāṃ mahīpataud sthite citrarathe vīre kathaṃ kṛṣṇas tvayārcitaḥd bāhlīkaṃ sthaviraṃ vīraṃ kauravāṇāṃ mahārathamd saumadattiṃ mahāvīryaṃ somadattaṃ mahārathamd śakuniṃ saubalaṃ caiva sindhurājaṃ mahābalamd etān avamatān kṛtvā kathaṃ kṛṣṇo rcitas tvayāa naiva ṛtviṅ na cācāryo na rājā madhusūdanaḥb na snātako na jāmātā kathaṃ kṛṣṇo rcitas tvayāc arcitaś ca kuruśreṣṭha kim anyat priyakāmyayāa atha vāpy arcanīyo yaṃ yuṣmākaṃ madhusūdanaḥc kiṃ rājabhir ihānītair avamānāya bhārataa vayaṃ tu na bhayād asya kaunteyasya mahātmanaḥc prayacchāmaḥ karān sarve na lobhān na ca sāntvanāta asya dharmapravṛttasya pārthivatvaṃ cikīrṣataḥc karān asmai prayacchāmaḥ so yam asmān na manyatea kim anyad avamānād dhi yad imaṃ rājasaṃsadic aprāptalakṣaṇaṃ kṛṣṇam arghyeṇārcitavān asia akasmād dharmaputrasya dharmātmeti yaśo gatamc ko hi dharmacyute pūjām evaṃ yuktāṃ prayojayete yo yaṃ vṛṣṇikule jāto rājānaṃ hatavān purāf jarāsaṃdhaṃ mahātmānam anyāyena durātmavāna adya dharmātmatā caiva vyapakṛṣṭā yudhiṣṭhirātc kṛpaṇatvaṃ niviṣṭaṃ ca kṛṣṇe rghyasya nivedanāta yadi bhītāś ca kaunteyāḥ kṛpaṇāś ca tapasvinaḥb rājñāṃ tu madhye pūjāṃ te kṛtavanto garīyasīmc nanu tvayāpi boddhavyaṃ yāṃ pūjāṃ mādhavo rhatia atha vā kṛpaṇair etām upanītāṃ janārdanac pūjām anarhaḥ kasmāt tvam abhyanujñātavān asia ayuktām ātmanaḥ pūjāṃ tvaṃ punar bahu manyasec haviṣaḥ prāpya niṣyandaṃ prāśituṃ śveva nirjanea na tv ayaṃ pārthivendrāṇām avamānaḥ prayujyatec tvām eva kuravo vyaktaṃ pralambhante janārdanaa klībe dārakriyā yādṛg andhe vā rūpadarśanamc arājño rājavat pūjā tathā te madhusūdanaa dṛṣṭo yudhiṣṭhiro rājā dṛṣṭo bhīṣmaś ca yādṛśaḥc vāsudevo py ayaṃ dṛṣṭaḥ sarvam etad yathātathama ity uktvā śiśupālas tān utthāya paramāsanātc niryayau sadasas tasmāt sahito rājabhis tadā vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā śiśupālam upādravatc uvāca cainaṃ madhuraṃ sāntvapūrvam idaṃ vacaḥa nedaṃ yuktaṃ mahīpāla yādṛśaṃ vai tvam uktavānc adharmaś ca paro rājan pāruṣyaṃ ca nirarthakama na hi dharmaṃ paraṃ jātu nāvabudhyeta pārthivac bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavas tv enaṃ māvamaṃsthā ato nyathāa paśya cemān mahīpālāṃs tvatto vṛddhatamān bahūnc mṛṣyante cārhaṇāṃ kṛṣṇe tadvat tvaṃ kṣantum arhasia veda tattvena kṛṣṇaṃ hi bhīṣmaś cedipate bhṛśamc na hy enaṃ tvaṃ tathā vettha yathainaṃ veda kauravaḥ bhīṣma uvācaa nāsmā anunayo deyo nāyam arhati sāntvanamc lokavṛddhatame kṛṣṇe yo rhaṇāṃ nānumanyatea kṣatriyaḥ kṣatriyaṃ jitvā raṇe raṇakṛtāṃ varaḥc yo muñcati vaśe kṛtvā gurur bhavati tasya saḥa asyāṃ ca samitau rājñām ekam apy ajitaṃ yudhic na paśyāmi mahīpālaṃ sātvatīputratejasāa na hi kevalam asmākam ayam arcyatamo cyutaḥc trayāṇām api lokānām arcanīyo janārdanaḥa kṛṣṇena hi jitā yuddhe bahavaḥ kṣatriyarṣabhāḥc jagat sarvaṃ ca vārṣṇeye nikhilena pratiṣṭhitama tasmāt satsv api vṛddheṣu kṛṣṇam arcāma netarānc evaṃ vaktuṃ na cārhas tvaṃ mā bhūt te buddhir īdṛśīa jñānavṛddhā mayā rājan bahavaḥ paryupāsitāḥb yasya rājan prabhāvajñāḥ purā sarve ca rakṣitāḥc teṣāṃ kathayatāṃ śaurer ahaṃ guṇavato guṇāne samāgatānām aśrauṣaṃ bahūn bahumatān satāma karmāṇy api ca yāny asya janmaprabhṛti dhīmataḥc bahuśaḥ kathyamānāni narair bhūyaḥ śrutāni mea na kevalaṃ vayaṃ kāmāc cedirāja janārdanamc na saṃbandhaṃ puraskṛtya kṛtārthaṃ vā kathaṃ canaa arcāmahe rcitaṃ sadbhir bhuvi bhaumasukhāvahamc yaśaḥ śauryaṃ jayaṃ cāsya vijñāyārcāṃ prayujmahea na hi kaś cid ihāsmābhiḥ subālo py aparīkṣitaḥc guṇair vṛddhān atikramya harir arcyatamo mataḥa jñānavṛddho dvijātīnāṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ balādhikaḥb vaiśyānāṃ dhānyadhanavāñ śūdrāṇām eva janmataḥc pūjye tāv iha govinde hetū dvāv api saṃsthitaua vedavedāṅgavijñānaṃ balaṃ cāpy amitaṃ tathāc nṛṇāṃ hi loke kasyāsti viśiṣṭaṃ keśavād ṛtea dānaṃ dākṣyaṃ śrutaṃ śauryaṃ hrīḥ kīrtir buddhir uttamāc saṃnatiḥ śrīr dhṛtis tuṣṭiḥ puṣṭiś ca niyatācyutea tam imaṃ sarvasaṃpannam ācāryaṃ pitaraṃ gurumc arcyam arcitam arcārhaṃ sarve saṃmantum arhathaa ṛtvig gurur vivāhyaś ca snātako nṛpatiḥ priyaḥc sarvam etad dhṛṣīkeśe tasmād abhyarcito cyutaḥa kṛṣṇa eva hi lokānām utpattir api cāpyayaḥc kṛṣṇasya hi kṛte bhūtam idaṃ viśvaṃ samarpitama eṣa prakṛtir avyaktā kartā caiva sanātanaḥc paraś ca sarvabhūtebhyas tasmād vṛddhatamo cyutaḥa buddhir mano mahān vāyus tejo mbhaḥ khaṃ mahī ca yāc caturvidhaṃ ca yad bhūtaṃ sarvaṃ kṛṣṇe pratiṣṭhitama ādityaś candramāś caiva nakṣatrāṇi grahāś ca yec diśaś copadiśaś caiva sarvaṃ kṛṣṇe pratiṣṭhitamd agnihotramukhā vedā gāyatrī chandasāṃ mukhamd rājā mukhaṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ nadīnāṃ sāgaro mukhamd nakṣatrāṇāṃ mukhaṃ candra ādityas tejasāṃ mukhamd parvatānāṃ mukhaṃ merur garuḍaḥ patatāṃ mukhamd ūrdhvaṃ tiryag adhaś caiva yāvatī jagato gatiḥd sadevakeṣu lokeṣu bhagavān keśavo mukhamd eṣa rudraś ca sarvātmā brahmā caiṣa sanātanaḥd akṣaraḥ kṣararūpeṇa mānuṣatvam upāgataḥa ayaṃ tu puruṣo bālaḥ śiśupālo na budhyatec sarvatra sarvadā kṛṣṇaṃ tasmād evaṃ prabhāṣatea yo hi dharmaṃ vicinuyād utkṛṣṭaṃ matimān naraḥc sa vai paśyed yathādharmaṃ na tathā cedirāḍ ayama savṛddhabāleṣv atha vā pārthiveṣu mahātmasuc ko nārhaṃ manyate kṛṣṇaṃ ko vāpy enaṃ na pūjayeta athemāṃ duṣkṛtāṃ pūjāṃ śiśupālo vyavasyatic duṣkṛtāyāṃ yathānyāyaṃ tathāyaṃ kartum arhatid vaiśaṃpāyanaḥd evam ukte tu gāṅgeye śiśupālaś cukopa had sahadevaḥd kruddhaṃ sunīthaṃ dṛṣṭvātha sahadevo bravīt tadād nītipūrvam idaṃ sarvaṃ cedirāja mayā kṛtamd na me vimatir astīha kāraṇaṃ cātra me śṛṇud sa pārthivānāṃ sarveṣāṃ guruḥ kṛṣṇo balena vaid tasmād abhyarcito rghyārhaḥ sarve saṃmantum arhathad yo vā na sahate rājñāṃ kaś cit sabalavāhanaḥd kṣipraṃ yuddhāya niryātu śaktaś ced atra me yudhid tasya mūrdhni susaṃnyastaṃ rājñaḥ savyaṃ padaṃ mayād evam ukto mayā hetur uttaraṃ prabravītu med vaiśaṃpāyanaḥd tato na vyājahāraiṣāṃ kaś cid buddhimatāṃ satāmd mānināṃ balināṃ rājñāṃ madhye saṃdarśite paded puṣpavṛṣṭir mahaty āsīt sahadevasya mūrdhanid evam ukte sunīthasya sahadevena keśaved svabhāvarakte nayane bhūyo rakte babhūvatuḥd tasya kopaṃ samudbhūtaṃ jñātvā bhīṣmaḥ pratāpavānd ācacakṣe punas tasmai kṛṣṇasyaivottamān guṇānd sa sunīthaṃ samāmantrya tāṃś ca sarvān mahīkṣitaḥd uvāca vadatāṃ śreṣṭha idaṃ matimatāṃ varaḥd sahadevena rājāno yad uktaṃ keśavaṃ pratid vaiśaṃpāyanaḥd tat tatheti vijānīdhvaṃ bhūyaś cātra nibodhatad tato bhīṣmasya tac chrutvā vacaḥ kāle yudhiṣṭhiraḥd uvāca matimān bhīṣmaṃ tataḥ kauravanandanaḥd vistareṇāsya devasya karmāṇīcchāmi sarvaśaḥd śrotuṃ bhagavatas tāni prabravīhi pitāmahad karmaṇām ānupūrvyaṃ ca prādurbhāvāṃś ca me vibhoḥd vaiśaṃpāyanaḥd yathā ca prakṛtiḥ kṛṣṇe tan me brūhi pitāmahad evam uktas tadā bhīṣmaḥ provāca puruṣarṣabhamd yudhiṣṭhiram amitraghnaṃ tasmin kṣatrasamāgamed samakṣaṃ vāsudevasya devasyeva śatakratoḥd karmāṇy asukarāṇy anyair ācacakṣe janādhipad śṛṇvatāṃ pārthivānāṃ ca dharmarājasya cāntiked idaṃ matimatāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ prati viśāṃ pated sāmnaivāmantrya rājendraṃ cedirājam ariṃdamamd bhīmakarmā tato bhīṣmo bhūyaḥ sa idam abravītd bhīṣmaḥd kurūṇāṃ cāpi rājānaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram uvāca had vartamānām atītāṃ ca śṛṇu rājan yudhiṣṭhirad īśvarasyottamasyaināṃ karmaṇāṃ gahanāṃ gatimd avyakto vyaktaliṅgastho ya eṣa bhagavān prabhuḥd purā nārāyaṇo devaḥ svayaṃbhūḥ prapitāmahaḥd sahasraśīrṣaḥ puruṣo dhruvo vyaktaḥ sanātanaḥd sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrāsyaḥ sahasracaraṇo vibhuḥd sahasrabāhuḥ sāhasro devo nāmasahasravānd sahasramukuṭo devo viśvarūpo mahādyutiḥd anekavarṇo devādir avyaktād vai pare sthitaḥd asṛjat salilaṃ pūrvaṃ sa ca nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥd tatas tu bhagavāṃs toye brahmāṇam asṛjat svayamd brahmā caturmukho lokān sarvāṃs tān asṛjat svayamd ādikāle purā hy evaṃ sarvalokasya codbhavaḥd purātha pralaye prāpte naṣṭe sthāvarajaṅgamed brahmādiṣu pralīneṣu naṣṭe loke carācared ābhūtasaṃplave prāpte pralīne prakṛtau mahānd ekas tiṣṭhati sarvātmā sa tu nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥd nārāyaṇasya cāṅgāni sarvadaivāni bhāratad śiras tasya divaṃ rājan nābhiḥ khaṃ caraṇau mahīd aśvinau karṇayor devau cakṣuṣī śaśibhāskaraud indravaiśvānarau devau mukhaṃ tasya mahātmanaḥd anyāni sarvadaivāni tasyāṅgāni mahātmanaḥd sarvaṃ vyāpya haris tasthau sūtraṃ maṇigaṇān ivad ābhūtasaṃplavānte tha dṛṣṭvā sarvaṃ tamonvitamd nārāyaṇo mahāyogī sarvajñaḥ paramātmavānd brahmabhūtas tadātmānaṃ brahmāṇam asṛjat svayamd so dhyakṣaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ prabhūtaḥ prabhavo cyutaḥd sanatkumāraṃ rudraṃ ca manuṃ caiva tapodhanānd sarvam evāsṛjad brahmā tato lokān prajās tathād tena tad vyasṛjat tatra prāpte kāle yudhiṣṭhirad tebhyo bhavan mahātmabhyo bahudhā brahma śāśvatamd kalpānāṃ bahukoṭyaś ca samatītā hi bhāratad ābhūtasaṃplavāś caiva bahukoṭyo ticakramuḥd manvantarayuge jasraṃ saṃkalpā bhūtasaṃplavāḥd cakravat parivartante sarvaṃ viṣṇumayaṃ jagatd sṛṣṭvā caturmukhaṃ devaṃ devo nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥd sa lokānāṃ hitārthāya kṣīrode vasati prabhuḥd brahmā tu sarvabhūtānāṃ lokasya ca pitāmahaḥd bhīṣmaḥd tato nārāyaṇo devaḥ sarvasya prapitāmahaḥd avyakto vyaktaliṅgastho ya eṣa bhagavān prabhuḥd nārāyaṇo jagac cakre prabhavāpyayasaṃhitaḥd eṣa nārāyaṇo bhūtvā harir āsīd yudhiṣṭhirad brahmāṇaṃ śaśisūryau ca dharmaṃ caivāsṛjat svayamd bahuśaḥ sarvabhūtātmā prādurbhavati kāryataḥd prādurbhāvāṃs tu vakṣyāmi divyān devagaṇair yutānd suptvā yugasahasraṃ sa prādurbhavati kāryavānd pūrṇe yugasahasre tha devadevo jagatpatiḥd brahmāṇaṃ kapilaṃ caiva parameṣṭhiṃ tathaiva cad devān saptaṛṣīṃś caiva śaṃkaraṃ ca mahāyaśāḥd sanatkumāraṃ bhagavān manuṃ caiva prajāpatimd purā cakre tha devādiḥ pradīptāgnisamaprabhaḥd yena cārṇavamadhyasthau naṣṭe sthāvarajaṅgamed naṣṭadevāsuranare praṇaṣṭoragarākṣased yoddhukāmau sudurdharṣau bhrātarau madhukaiṭabhaud hatau prabhavatā tena tayor dattvā vṛtaṃ varamd bhūmiṃ baddhvā kṛtau pūrvaṃ mṛnmayau dvau mahāsuraud karṇasrotodbhavau tau tu viṣṇos tasya mahātmanaḥd mahārṇave prasvapataḥ śailarājasamau sthitaud tau viveśa svayaṃ vāyur brahmaṇā sādhu coditaḥd tau divaṃ chādayitvā tu vavṛdhāte mahāsuraud vāyuprāṇau tu tau dṛṣṭvā brahmā paryāmṛśac chanaiḥd ekaṃ mṛdutaraṃ viddhi kaṭhinaṃ viddhi cāparamd nāmanī tu tayoś cakre sa vibhuḥ salilodbhavaḥd mṛdus tv ayaṃ madhur nāma kaṭhinaḥ kaiṭabhaḥ svayamd tau daityau kṛtanāmānau ceratur balagarvitaud tau purātha divaṃ sarvāṃ prāptau rājan mahāsuraud pracchādyātha divaṃ sarvāṃ ceratur madhukaiṭabhaud sarvam ekārṇavaṃ lokaṃ yoddhukāmau sunirbhayaud tau gatāv asurau dṛṣṭvā brahmā lokapitāmahaḥd ekārṇavāmbunicaye tatraivāntaradhīyatad sa padme padmanābhasya nābhideśāt samutthited āsīd ādau svayaṃ janma tat paṅkajam apaṅkajamd pūjayām āsa vasatiṃ brahmā lokapitāmahaḥd tāv ubhau jalagarbhasthau nārāyaṇacaturmukhaud bahūn varṣāyutān apsu śayānau na cakampatuḥd atha dīrghasya kālasya tāv ubhau madhukaiṭabhaud ājagmatus tam uddeśaṃ yatra brahmā vyavasthitaḥd tau dṛṣṭvā lokanāthas tu kopāt saṃraktalocanaḥd utpapātātha śayanāt padmanābho mahādyutiḥd tad yuddham abhavad ghoraṃ tayos tasya ca vai tadād ekārṇave tadā ghore trailokye jalatāṃ gated tad abhūt tumulaṃ yuddhaṃ varṣasaṃghān sahasraśaḥd na ca tāv asurau yuddhe tadā śramam avāpatuḥd atha dīrghasya kālasya tau daityau yuddhadurmadaud ūcatuḥ prītamanasau devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ prabhumd prītau svas tava yuddhena ślāghyas tvaṃ mṛtyur āvayoḥd āvāṃ jahi na yatrorvī salilena pariplutād hatau ca tava putratvaṃ prāpnuyāva surottamad yo hy āvāṃ yudhi nirjetā tasyāvāṃ vihitau sutaud tayoḥ sa vacanaṃ śrutvā tadā nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥd tau pragṛhya mṛdhe daityau dorbhyāṃ tau samapīḍayatd ūrubhyāṃ nidhanaṃ cakre tāv ubhau madhukaiṭabhaud tau hatau cāplutau toye vapurbhyām ekatāṃ gataud medo mumucatur daityau mathyamānau jalormibhiḥd medasā taj jalaṃ vyāptaṃ tābhyām antardadhe tadād nārāyaṇaś ca bhagavān asṛjad vividhāḥ prajāḥd daityayor medasā channā sarvā rājan vasuṃdharād tadā prabhṛti kaunteya medinīti smṛtā mahīd prabhāvāt padmanābhasya śāśvatī ca kṛtā nṛṇāmd bhīṣmaḥd prādurbhāvasahasrāṇi samatītāny anekaśaḥd yathāśakti tu vakṣyāmi śṛṇu tān kurunandanad purā kamalanābhasya svapataḥ sāgarāmbhasid puṣkare yatra saṃbhūtā devā ṛṣigaṇaiḥ sahad eṣa pauṣkariko nāma prādurbhāvaḥ prakīrtitaḥd purāṇaḥ kathyate yatra vedaśrutisamāhitaḥd vārāhas tu śrutimukhaḥ prādurbhāvo mahātmanaḥd yatra viṣṇuḥ suraśreṣṭho vārāhaṃ rūpam āsthitaḥd ujjahāra mahīṃ toyāt saśailavanakānanāmd vedapādo yūpadaṃṣṭraḥ kratudantaś citīmukhaḥd agnijihvo darbharomā brahmaśīrṣo mahātapāḥd ahorātrekṣaṇo divyo vedāṅgaḥ śrutibhūṣaṇaḥd ājyanāsaḥ snuvatuṇḍaḥ sāmaghoṣasvano mahānd dharmasatyamayaḥ śrīmān karmavikramasatkṛtaḥd prāyaścittamayo dhīraḥ paśujānur mahāvṛṣaḥd udgātṛhomaliṅgo sau paśubījamahauṣadhiḥd bāhyāntarātmā mantrāsthivikṛtaḥ saumyadarśanaḥd vedaskandho havirgandho havyakavyādivegavānd prāgvaṃśakāyo dyutimān nānādīkṣābhir ācitaḥd dakṣiṇāhṛdayo yogī mahāsatramayo mahānd upākarmoṣṭharucakaḥ pravargyāvartabhūṣaṇaḥd chāyāpatnīsahāyo vai maṇiśṛṅga ivocchritaḥd evaṃ yajñavarāho vai bhūtvā viṣṇuḥ sanātanaḥd mahīṃ sāgaraparyantāṃ saśailavanakānanāmd ekārṇavajale bhraṣṭām ekārṇavagataḥ prabhuḥd majjitāṃ salile tasmin svadevīṃ pṛthivīṃ tadād ujjahāra viṣāṇena mārkaṇḍeyasya paśyataḥd śṛṅgeṇemāṃ samuddhṛtya lokānāṃ hitakāmyayād sahasraśīrṣo deveśo nirmame jagatīṃ prabhuḥd evaṃ yajñavarāheṇa bhūtabhavyabhavātmanād uddhṛtā pṛthivī devī sāgarāmbudharā purād nihatā dānavāḥ sarve devadevena viṣṇunād vārāhaḥ kathito hy eṣa nārasiṃham atho śṛṇud yatra bhūtvā mṛgendreṇa hiraṇyakaśipur hataḥd bhīṣmaḥd daityendro balavān rājan surārir balagarvitaḥd hiraṇyakaśipur nāma āsīt trailokyakaṇṭakaḥd daityānām ādipuruṣo vīryavān dhṛtimān balīd sa praviśya vanaṃ rājaṃś cakāra tapa uttamamd daśa varṣasahasrāṇi śatāni daśa pañca cad japopavāsas tasyāsīt sthāṇur maunavrato dṛḍhaḥd tato damaśamābhyāṃ ca brahmacaryeṇa cānaghad brahmā prītamanās tasya tapasā niyamena cad tataḥ svayaṃbhūr bhagavān svayam āgamya bhūpated vimānenārkavarṇena haṃsayuktena bhāsvatād ādityair vasubhiḥ sādhyair marudbhir daivataiḥ sahad radrair viśvasahāyaiś ca yakṣarākṣasakiṃnaraiḥd diśābhir vidiśābhiś ca nadībhiḥ sāgarais tathād nakṣatraiś ca muhūrtaiś ca khecaraiś cāparair grahaiḥd devarṣibhis tapoyuktaiḥ siddhaiḥ saptarṣibhis tathād rājarṣibhiḥ puṇyatamair gandharvair apsarogaṇaiḥd carācaraguruḥ śrīmān vṛtaḥ sarvasurais tathād brahmād brahmā brahmavidāṃ śreṣṭho daityam āgamya cābravītd prīto smi tava bhaktasya tapasānena suvratad varaṃ varaya bhadraṃ te yatheṣṭaṃ kāmam āpnuhid hiraṇyakaśipuḥd na devāsuragandharvā na yakṣoragarākṣasāḥd na mānuṣāḥ piśācāś ca hanyur māṃ devasattamad ṛṣayo vā na māṃ śāpaiḥ kruddhā lokapitāmahad śapeyus tapasā yuktā vara eṣa vṛto mayād na śastreṇa na cāstreṇa giriṇā pādapena cad na śuṣkeṇa na cārdreṇa syān na cānyena me vadhaḥd nākāśe vā na bhūmau vā rātrau vā divase pi vād nāntar vā na bahir vāpi syād vadho me pitāmahad paśubhir vā mṛgair na syāt pakṣibhir vā sarīsṛpaiḥd brahmād dadāsi ced varān etān devadeva vṛṇomy ahamd ete divyā varās tāta mayā dattās tavādbhutāḥd sarvakāmān varāṃs tāta prāpsyase tvaṃ na saṃśayaḥd evam uktvā sa bhagavān ākāśena jagāma had rarāja brahmaloke sa brahmarṣigaṇasevitaḥd tato devāś ca nāgāś ca gandharvā munayas tathād varapradānaṃ śrutvā te brahmāṇam upatasthired devāḥd vareṇānena bhagavan bādhiṣyati sa no suraḥd tat prasīdasva bhagavan vadho sya pravicintyatāmd bhagavan sarvabhūtānāṃ svayaṃbhūr ādikṛd vibhuḥd bhīṣmaḥd sraṣṭā ca havyakavyānām avyaktaprakṛtir dhruvaḥd tato lokahitaṃ vākyaṃ śrutvā devaḥ prajāpatiḥd provāca bhagavān vākyaṃ sarvadevagaṇāṃs tadād avaśyaṃ tridaśās tena prāptavyaṃ tapasaḥ phalamd tapaso nte sya bhagavān vadhaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ kariṣyatid etac chrutvā surāḥ sarve brahmaṇā tasya vai vadhamd svāni sthānāni divyāni jagmus te vai mudānvitāḥd labdhamātre vare cāpi sarvās tā bādhate prajāḥd hiraṇyakaśipur daityo varadānena darpitaḥd rājyaṃ cakāra daityendro daityasaṃghaiḥ samāvṛtaḥd sapta dvīpān vaśe cakre lokālokāntaraṃ balātd divyalokān samastān vai bhogān divyān avāpa saḥd devāṃs tribhuvanasthāṃs tān parājitya mahāsuraḥd trailokyaṃ vaśam ānīya svarge vasati dānavaḥd yadā varamadonmatto nyavasad dānavo divid atha lokān samastāṃś ca vijitya sa mahābalaḥd bhaveyam aham evendraḥ somo gnir māruto raviḥd salilaṃ cāntarikṣaṃ ca nakṣatrāṇi diśo daśad ahaṃ krodhaś ca kāmaś ca varuṇo vāsavo yamaḥd dhanadaś ca dhanādhyakṣo yakṣaḥ kiṃpuruṣādhipaḥd ete bhaveyam ity uktvā svayaṃ bhūtvā balāt sa cad teṣāṃ gṛhītvā sthānāni teṣāṃ kāryāṇy avāpa saḥd īḍyaś cāsmin makhavarair devakiṃnarasattamaiḥd narakasthān samānīya svargasthāṃs tāṃś cakāra saḥd evamādīni karmāṇi kṛtvā daityapatir balīd āśrameṣu mahābhāgān munīn vai saṃśitavratānd satyadharmaratān dāntān purā dharṣitavāṃś ca saḥd yajñīyān kṛtavān daityān ayajñīyāś ca devatāḥd yatra yatra surā jagmus tatra tatra vrajanty utad sthānāni devatānāṃ tu hṛtvā rājyam apālayatd pañca koṭyaś ca varṣāṇi niyutāny ekaṣaṣṭi cad ṣaṣṭiś caiva sahasrāṇāṃ jagmus tasya durātmanaḥd etad varṣaṃ sa daityendro bhogaiśvaryam avāpa saḥd tenāti bādhyamānās te daityendreṇa balīyasād brahmalokaṃ surā jagmuḥ sarve śakrapurogamāḥd devāḥd pitāmahaṃ samāsādya khinnāḥ prāñjalayo bruvand bhagavan bhūtabhavyeśa nas trāyasva ihāgatānd bhayaṃ ditisutād ghoraṃ bhavaty adya divāniśamd bhagavan sarvabhūtānāṃ svayaṃbhūr ādikṛd vibhuḥd brahmād sraṣṭā tvaṃ havyakavyānām avyaktaḥ prakṛtir dhruvaḥd śrūyatām āpad evaṃ hi durvijñeyaṃ mayāpi cad nārāyaṇas tu puruṣo viśvarūpo mahādyutiḥd avyaktaḥ sarvabhūtānām acintyo vibhur avyayaḥd mamāpi sa tu yuṣmākaṃ vyasane paramā gatiḥd nārāyaṇaḥ paro vyaktād aham avyaktasaṃbhavaḥd matto jajñuḥ prajā lokāḥ sarvadevāsurāś ca ted devā yathāhaṃ yuṣmākaṃ tathā nārāyaṇo mamad pitāmaho haṃ sarvasya sa viṣṇuḥ prapitāmahaḥd niścitaṃ vibudhā daityaṃ sa viṣṇus taṃ haniṣyatid bhīṣmaḥd tasya nāsti hy aśakyaṃ ca tasmād vrajata māciramd pitāmahavacaḥ śrutvā sarve te bharatarṣabhad vibudhā brahmaṇā sārdhaṃ jagmuḥ kṣīrodadhiṃ pratid ādityā vasavaḥ sādhyā viśve ca marutas tathād rudrā maharṣayaś caiva aśvinau ca surūpiṇaud anye ca divyā ye rājaṃs te sarve sagaṇāḥ surāḥd caturmukhaṃ puraskṛtya śvetadvīpam upasthitāḥd gatvā kṣīrasamudre taṃ śāśvatīṃ paramāṃ gatimd anantaśayanaṃ devam anantaṃ dīptatejasamd śaraṇyaṃ tridaśā viṣṇum upatasthuḥ sanātanamd devaṃ brahmamayaṃ yajñaṃ brahmadevaṃ mahābalamd bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyac ca prabhuṃ lokanamaskṛtamd devāḥd nārāyaṇaṃ vibhuṃ devaṃ śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥd trāyasva no dya deveśa hiraṇyakaśipor vadhātd tvaṃ hi naḥ paramo dhātā brahmādīnāṃ surottamad utphullāmalapatrākṣa śatrupakṣabhayaṃkarad kṣayāya ditivaṃśasya śaraṇaṃ tvaṃ bhaviṣyasid bhīṣmaḥd devānāṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā tadā viṣṇuḥ śuciśravāḥd viṣṇuḥd adṛśyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ vaktum evopacakramed bhayaṃ tyajadhvam amarā abhayaṃ vo dadāmy ahamd tad evaṃ tridivaṃ devāḥ pratipadyata māciramd eṣo haṃ sagaṇaṃ daityaṃ varadānena darpitamd brahmād avadhyam amarendrāṇāṃ dānavendraṃ nihanmy ahamd bhagavan bhūtabhavyeśa khinnā hy ete bhṛśaṃ surāḥd viṣṇuḥd tasmāt tvaṃ jahi daityendraṃ kṣipraṃ kālo sya mā ciramd kṣipraṃ devāḥ kariṣyāmi tvarayā daityanāśanamd tasmāt tvaṃ vibudhāś caiva pratipadyata vai divamd bhīṣmaḥd evam uktvā tu bhagavān visṛjya tridiveśvarānd narasyārdhatanuṃ kṛtvā siṃhasyārdhatanuṃ tathād nārasiṃhena vapuṣā pāṇiṃ niṣpiṣya pāṇinād bhīmarūpo mahātejā vyāditāsya ivāntakaḥd hiraṇyakaśipuṃ rājañ jagāma harir īśvaraḥd daityās tam āgataṃ dṛṣṭvā nārasiṃhaṃ mahābalamd vavarṣuḥ śastravarṣais te susaṃkruddhās tadā harimd tair visṛṣṭāni śastrāṇi bhakṣayām āsa vai hariḥd jaghāna ca raṇe daityān sahasrāṇi bahūny apid tān nihatya ca daityendrān sarvān kruddhān mahābalānd abhyadhāvat susaṃkruddho daityendraṃ balagarvitamd jīmūtaghanasaṃkāśo jīmūtaghananisvanaḥd jīmūta iva dīptaujā jīmūta iva vegavānd devārir ditijo duṣṭo nṛsiṃhaṃ samupādravatd daityaṃ so tibalaṃ dṛṣṭvā kruddhaśārdūlavikramamd dṛptair daityagaṇair guptaṃ kharair nakhamukhair utad tataḥ kṛtvā tu yuddhaṃ vai tena daityena vai hariḥd saṃdhyākāle mahātejā bhavanānte tvarānvitaḥd ūrau nidhāya daityendraṃ nirbibheda nakhair hi tamd mahābalaṃ mahāvīryaṃ varadānena darpitamd daityaśreṣṭhaṃ suraśreṣṭho jaghāna tarasā hariḥd hiraṇyakaśipuṃ hatvā sarvān daityāṃś ca vai tadād vibudhānāṃ prajānāṃ ca hitaṃ kṛtvā mahādyutiḥd pramumoda harir devaḥ prāpya dharmaṃ tadā bhuvid eṣa te nārasiṃho tra kathitaḥ pāṇḍunandanad bhīṣmaḥd śṛṇu tvaṃ vāmanaṃ nāma prādurbhāvaṃ mahātmanaḥd purā tretāyuge rājan balir vairocano bhavatd daityānāṃ pārthivo vīro balenāpratimo balīd tadā balir mahārāja daityasaṃghaiḥ samāvṛtaḥd vijitya tarasā śakram indrasthānam avāpa saḥd tena vitrāsitā devā balinākhaṇḍalādayaḥd brahmāṇaṃ vai puraskṛtya gatvā kṣīrodadhiṃ tadād tuṣṭuvuḥ sahitāḥ sarve devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ prabhumd teṣāṃ prasādaṃ cakre tha vibudhānāṃ haris tadād prasādajaṃ tasya vibhor adityāṃ janma ucyated aditer api putratvam etya yādavanandanaḥd eṣa viṣṇur iti khyāta indrasyāvarajo bhavatd tasminn eva tu kāle tu daityendro vīryavān balīd aśvamedhaṃ kratuśreṣṭham āhartum upacakramed vartamāne tadā yajñe daityendrasya yudhiṣṭhirad sa viṣṇur vāmano bhūtvā pracchanno brahmaveṣadhṛkd muṇḍo yajñopavītī ca kṛṣṇājinadharaḥ śikhīd palāśadaṇḍaṃ saṃgṛhya vāmano dbhutadarśanaḥd praviśya sa baler yajñe vartamāne tu dakṣiṇāmd dehīty uvāca daityendraṃ vikramāṃs trīn mamaiva had dīyatāṃ tripadīmātram ity avocan mahāsuramd sa tatheti pratiśrutya pradadau viṣṇave tadād tena labdhvā harir bhūmiṃ jṛmbhayām āsa vai bhṛśamd sa śiśuḥ sadivaṃ khaṃ ca pṛthivīṃ ca viśāṃ pated tribhir vikramaṇair etat sarvam ākramatābhibhūḥd baler balavato yajñe balinā viṣṇunā purād vikramais tribhir akṣobhyāḥ kṣobhitās te mahāsurāḥd vipracittimukhāḥ kruddhā daityasaṃghā mahābalāḥd nānāvaktrā mahākāyā nānāveṣadharā nṛpad nānāpraharaṇā raudrā nānāmālyānulepanāḥd svāny āyudhāni saṃgṛhya pradīptā iva tejasād kramamāṇaṃ hariṃ tatra upāvartanta bhāratad pramathya sarvān daiteyān pādahastatalais tu tānd rūpaṃ kṛtvā mahābhīmaṃ jahārāśu sa medinīmd saṃprāpya divam ākāśam ādityasadane sthitaḥd atyarocata bhūtātmā bhāskaraṃ svena tejasād prakāśayan diśaḥ sarvāḥ pradiśaś ca mahābalaḥd śuśubhe sa mahābāhuḥ sarvalokān prakāśayand tasya vikramato bhūmiṃ candrādityau stanāntared nabhaḥ prakramamāṇasya nābhyāṃ kila tadā sthitaud param ākramamāṇasya jānubhyāṃ tau vyavasthitaud viṣṇor amitavīryasya vadanty evaṃ dvijātayaḥd athāsādya kapālaṃ sa aṇḍasya tu yudhiṣṭhirad tacchidrāt syandinī tasya pādād bhraṣṭātha nimnagād sasāra sāgaraṃ sāśu pāvanī sāgaraṃgamād jahāra medinīṃ sarvāṃ hatvā dānavapuṃgavānd āsurīṃ śriyam āhṛtya trīṃl lokān sa janārdanaḥd saputradārān asurān pātāle vinyapātayatd namuciḥ śambaraś caiva prahlādaś ca mahāmanāḥd pādapātābhinirdhūtāḥ pātāle vinipātitāḥd mahābhūtāni bhūtātmā saviśeṣāṇi vai hariḥd kālaṃ ca sakalaṃ rājan gātrabhūtāny adarśayatd tasya gātre jagat sarvam ānītam iva dṛśyated na kiṃ cid asti lokeṣu yad anāptaṃ mahātmanād tad sayakṣoragacāraṇānd te vadhyamānā daiteyair devasaṃghās tadā raṇed dudruvuḥ saṃpariśrāntāḥ kṣīṇapraharaṇā raṇed trātāraṃ manasā jagmur devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ prabhumd etasminn antare tatra jagāma harir daiteyadānavaiḥd tad yuddham abhavad ghoram acintyaṃ romaharṣaṇamd jaghnur daityān raṇe devāḥ sarve śakrapurogamāḥd te vadhyamānā vibudhair dudruvur daityadānavāḥd vidrutān dānavān dṛṣṭvā tadā bhārata saṃyuged kālanemir iti khyāto dānavaḥ pratyadṛśyatad śatapraharaṇo ghoraḥ śatabāhuḥ śatānanaḥd śataśīrṣaḥ sthitaḥ śrīmāñ śataśṛṅga ivācalaḥd bhāskarākāramukuṭaḥ śiñjitābharaṇāṅgadaḥd dhūmrakeśo hariśmaśrur nirdaṣṭhoṣṭhapuṭānanaḥd trailokyāntaravistāraṃ dhārayan vipulaṃ vapuḥd tarjayan vai raṇe devāñ chādayan sa diśo daśad abhyadhāvat susaṃkruddho vyāditāsya ivāntakaḥd tataḥ śastraprapātaiś ca devān dharṣitavān raṇed athābhyayuḥ surān sarvān punas te daityadānavāḥd āpīḍayan raṇe kruddhās tato devān yudhiṣṭhirad te vadhyamānā vibudhāḥ samare kālaneminād daityaiś caiva mahārāja dudruvuḥ sahitā diśaḥd vidrutān vibudhān dṛṣṭvā kālanemir mahāsuraḥd indraṃ yamāgnivaruṇān vāyuṃ ca dhanadaṃ ravimd etāṃś cānyān balāj jitvā teṣāṃ kāryāṇy avāpa saḥd tān sarvāṃs tarasā jitvā kālanemir mahāsuraḥd dadarśa gagane viṣṇuṃ suparṇasthaṃ mahādyutimd taṃ dṛṣṭvā krodhatāmrākṣas tarjayann abhyayāt tadād sa bāhuśatam udyamya sarvāstragrahaṇaṃ raṇed roṣād bhārata daityendro viṣṇor urasi pātayatd daityāś ca dānavāś caiva sarve mayapurogamāḥd svāny āyudhāni saṃgṛhya sarve viṣṇum atāḍayand sa tāḍyamāno tibalair daityaiḥ sarvāyudhodyataiḥd na cacāla harir yuddhe kampyamāna ivācalaḥd punar udyamya saṃkruddhaḥ kālanemir dṛḍhāṃ gadāmd jaghāna saṃyuge rājan sa viṣṇuṃ garuḍaṃ ca vaid sa dṛṣṭvā garuḍaṃ śrāntaṃ cakram udyamya vai hariḥd śataṃ śirāṃsi bāhūṃś ca so cchinat kālaneminaḥd jaghānānyāṃś ca tān sarvān samare daityadānavānd tasmin rājan raṇe daityās traya eva viniḥsṛtāḥd virocano mayaś caiva svarbhānuś ca mahāsuraḥd sarvān aśeṣān hatvā tu viṣṇur vai daityadānavānd vibudhānām ṛṣīṇāṃ ca svāni sthānāni vai dadaud dattvā surāṇāṃ suprītiṃ prāpya sarvāṇi bhāratad jagāma brahmaṇā sārdhaṃ brahmalokaṃ tadā hariḥd brahmalokaṃ praviśyātha tatra nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥd paurāṇāṃ guhyasadanaṃ divyaṃ nārāyaṇāśramamd saṃpraviśya tadā devaḥ stūyamāno maharṣibhiḥd sahasraśīrṣo bhūtvātha śayanāyopacakramed ādidevaḥ purāṇātmā nidrāvaśam upāgataḥd śete sukhaṃ sadā viṣṇur mohayañ jagad avyayaḥd jagmus tasyātha varṣāṇi śayānasya mahātmanaḥd ṣaṭtriṃśacchatasāhasraṃ mānuṣeṇeha saṃkhyayād tataḥ kṛtayugatretādvāparānte bubodha saḥd brahmādibhiḥ suraiś cāpi stūyamāno maharṣibhiḥd utplutya śayanād viṣṇur brahmaṇā vibudhaiḥ sahad devānāṃ ca hitārthāya yayau devasabhāṃ pratid meroḥ śikharavinyastāṃ jvalantīṃ tāṃ śubhāṃ sabhāmd viviśus tāṃ surāḥ sarve brahmaṇā saha bhāratad jagmus tatra niṣedus te sā niḥśabdam abhūt tadād bhūmiḥd tatra bhūmir uvācātha khedāt karuṇabhāṣiṇīd rājñāṃ balair balavatāṃ khinnāsmi bhṛśapīḍitād nityaṃ bhārapariśrāntā duḥkhāj jīvāmi vai surāḥd pure pure ca nṛpatiḥ koṭisaṃkhyair balair vṛtaḥd rāṣṭre rāṣṭre ca śataśo grāmāḥ kulasahasriṇaḥd bhūmipānāṃ sahasraiś ca teṣāṃ ca balināṃ balaiḥd grāmāyutaiś ca rāṣṭraiś ca ahaṃ nirvivarīkṛtād ke cid daityeṣu cotpannā ke cid rākṣasayonayaḥd tasmād dhārayituṃ śaktā na śakṣyāmi janān ahamd daityeśair bādhyamānās tāḥ prajā nityaṃ durātmabhiḥd bhīṣmaḥd bhūmes tad vacanaṃ śrutvā devo nārāyaṇas tadād bhīṣmaḥd vyādiśya tān surān sarvān kṣitau vastuṃ mano dadhed yac cakre bhagavān viṣṇur vasudevakulodbhavaḥd tat te haṃ nṛpa vakṣyāmi śṛṇu sarvam aśeṣataḥd vāsudevasya māhātmyaṃ caritaṃ ca mahādyuteḥd hitārthaṃ suramartyānāṃ lokānāṃ hi hitāya cad yadā divi vibhus tāta na reme bhagavān asaud tato vyādiśya bhūtāni bhuvi bhaumasukhāvahaḥd nigrahārthāya daityānāṃ codayām āsa vai tadād marutaś ca vasūṃś caiva sūryācandramasāv ubhaud gandharvāpsarasaś caiva rudrādityāṃs tathāśvinaud jāyadhvaṃ mānuṣe loke sarvabhūtamaheśvarāḥd jaṅgamāni viśālākṣo hy ātmānaṃ hy ātmanāsṛjatd jāyatām iti govindas tiryagyonigatair apid tāni sarvāṇi sarvajñaḥ sasurāṇi sureśvaraḥd ta evam uktāḥ kṛṣṇena sarva eva divaukasaḥd daityadānavahantāraḥ saṃbhūtā bhuvaneśvarāḥd yayātivaṃśajasyātha vasudevasya dhīmataḥd kule puṇyayaśaḥkarmā bheje nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥd ājñāpayitvā ratyartham ajāyata yadoḥ kuled ātmānam ātmanā tāta kṛtvā bahuvidhaṃ hariḥd ratyartham eva gāvas tā rarakṣa puruṣottamaḥd ajātaśatro jātas tu yathaiṣa bhuvi bhūmipad bhīṣmaḥd kīrtyamānaṃ mayā tāta nibodha bharatarṣabhad sāgarāḥ samakampanta mudā celuś ca parvatāḥd jajvaluś cāgnayaḥ śāntā jāyamāne janārdaned śivāḥ saṃpravavur vātāḥ praśāntam abhavad rajaḥd jyotīṃṣi saṃprakāśante jāyamāne janārdaned devadundubhayaś cāpi sasvanur bhṛśam ambared abhyavarṣat tadāgamya nāradaḥ puṣpavṛṣṭibhiḥd gīrbhir maṅgalayuktābhir astuvan madhusūdanamd upatasthus tadā prītāḥ prādurbhāve maharṣayaḥd tatas tān abhisaṃprekṣya nāradapramukhān ṛṣīnd upānṛtyann upajagur gandharvāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥd upatasthe ca govindaṃ sahasrākṣaḥ śacīpatiḥd abhyabhāṣata tejasvī maharṣīn pūjayaṃs tadād kṛtyāni devakāryāṇi kṛtvā lokahitāya cad svaṃ lokaṃ lokakṛd devaḥ punar gacchati tejasād ity uktvā munibhiḥ sārdhaṃ jagāma tridiveśvaraḥd abhyanujñāya tān sarvāñ chādayan prakṛtiṃ parāmd nandagopakule kṛṣṇa uṣitvā bahulāḥ samāḥd vasudevas tato jātaṃ bālam ādityasaṃnibhamd nandagopakule rājan bhayāt pracchādayad dharimd tataḥ kadācit suptaṃ taṃ śakaṭasya tv adhaḥ śiśumd yaśodā saṃparityajya jagāma yamunāṃ nadīmd śiśulīlāṃ tataḥ kurvan svahastacaraṇau kṣipand ruroda madhuraṃ kṛṣṇaḥ pādāv ūrdhvaṃ prasārayand pādāṅguṣṭhena śakaṭaṃ dhārayann atha keśavaḥd tatrāthaikena pādena pātayitvā tadā śiśuḥd nyubjaṃ payodharākāṅkṣī cakāra ca ruroda cad pātitaṃ śakaṭaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhinnabhāṇḍaghaṭīghaṭamd janās te śiśunā tena vismayaṃ paramaṃ yayuḥd pratyakṣaṃ śūrasenānāṃ dṛśyate mahad adbhutamd śayānena hataḥ pakṣī śiśunā tigmatejasād pūtanā cāpi nihatā mahākāyā mahāstanīd paśyatāṃ sarvadevānāṃ vāsudevena bhāratad tataḥ kāle mahārāja saṃsaktau rāmakeśavaud kṛṣṇaḥ saṃkarṣaṇaś cobhau riṅkhiṇau samapadyatāmd anyonyakiraṇagrastau candrasūryāv ivāmbared visarpayetāṃ sarvatra sarpabhogabhujau tadād rejatuḥ pāṃsudigdhāṅgau rāmakṛṣṇau tadā nṛpad kva cic ca jānubhiḥ spṛṣṭau krīḍamānau kva cid vaned pibantau dadhikulyāś ca mathyamāne ca bhāratad tataḥ sa bālo govindo navanītaṃ tadākṣayamd grasamānas tu tatrātha gopībhir dadṛśe tha vaid dāmnātholūkhale kṛṣṇo gopastrībhiś ca bandhitaḥd tadātha śiśunā tena rājaṃs tāv arjunāv ubhaud samūlaviṭapau bhagnau tad adbhutam ivābhavatd tatas tau bālyam uttīrṇau kṛṣṇasaṃkarṣaṇāv ubhaud tasminn eva vrajasthāne saptavarṣau babhūvatuḥd nīlapītāmbaradharau pītaśvetānulepanaud babhūvatur vatsapālau kākapakṣadharāv ubhaud parṇavādyaṃ śrutisukhaṃ vādayantau varānanaud śuśubhāte vanagatāv udīrṇāv iva pannagaud mayūrāṅgajakarṇau tau pallavāpīḍadhāriṇaud vanamālāparikṣiptau sālapotāv ivodgataud aravindakṛtāpīḍau rajjuyajñopavītinaud śikyatumbadharau vīrau gopaveṇupravādakaud kva cid dhasantāv anyonyaṃ krīḍamānau kva cid vaned parṇaśayyāsu saṃsuptau kva cin nidrāntaraiṣiṇaud tau vatsān pālayantau hi śobhayantau mahad vanamd cañcūryantau ramantau sma rājann evaṃ tadā śubhaud tato vṛndāvanaṃ gatvā vasudevasutāv ubhaud bhīṣmaḥd govrajaṃ tatra kaunteya cārayantau vijahratuḥd tataḥ kadā cid govindo jyeṣṭhaṃ saṃkarṣaṇaṃ vinād cacāra tad vanaṃ ramyaṃ ramyarūpo varānanaḥd kākapakṣadharaḥ śrīmāñ cid gāyan kva cit krīḍan kva cin nṛtyan kva cid dhasand gopaveṇuṃ sa madhuraṃ kāmaṃ tad api vādayand prahlādanārthaṃ tu gavāṃ kva cid vanagato yuvād gokule meghakāle tu cacāra dyutimān prabhuḥd bahuramyeṣu deśeṣu vanasya vanarājiṣud tāsu kṛṣṇo mudaṃ lebhe krīḍayā bharatarṣabhad sa kadā cid vane tasmin gobhiḥ saha parivrajand bhāṇḍīraṃ nāma dṛṣṭvātha nyagrodhaṃ keśavo mahānd tasya chāyānivāsāya matiṃ cakre tadā prabhuḥd sa tatra vayasā tulyair vatsapālaiḥ sahānaghad reme sa divasān kṛṣṇaḥ purā svargapure yathād taṃ krīḍamānaṃ gopālāḥ kṛṣṇaṃ bhāṇḍīravāsinaḥd ramayanti sma bahavo mānyaiḥ krīḍanakais tadād anye sma parigāyanti gopā muditamānasāḥd gopālāḥ kṛṣṇam evānye gāyanti sma vanapriyāḥd teṣāṃ sa gāyatām eva vādayām āsa keśavaḥd parṇavādyāntare veṇuṃ tumbavīṇāṃ ca tatra vaid evaṃ krīḍāntaraiḥ kṛṣṇo gopālair vijahāra saḥd tena bālena kaunteya kṛtaṃ lokahitaṃ tadād paśyatāṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ vāsudevena bhāratad hrade nīpavane tatra krīḍitaṃ nāgamūrdhanid śāsayitvā tu kālīyaṃ sarvalokasya paśyataḥd vijahāra tataḥ kṛṣṇo baladevasahāyavānd dhenuko dāruṇo daityo rājan rāsabhavigrahaḥd tadā tālavane rājan baladevena vai hataḥd tataḥ kadā cit kaunteya rāmakṛṣṇau vanaṃ gataud cārayantau pravṛddhāni godhanāni śubhānanaud viharantau mudā yuktau vīkṣamāṇau vanāni vaid kṣvelayantau pragāyantau vicinvantau ca pādapānd nāmabhir vyāharantau ca vatsān gāś ca paraṃtapaud ceratur lokasiddhābhiḥ krīḍābhir aparājitaud tau devau mānuṣīṃ dīkṣāṃ vahantau surapūjitaud tajjātiguṇayuktābhiḥ krīḍābhiś ceratur vanamd tataḥ kṛṣṇo mahātejās tadā gatvā tu govrajamd giriyajñaṃ tam evaiṣa prakṛtaṃ gopadārakaiḥd bubhuje pāyasaṃ śaurir īśvaraḥ sarvabhūtakṛtd taṃ dṛṣṭvā gopakāḥ sarve kṛṣṇam eva samarcayand pūjyamānas tato gopair divyaṃ vapur adhārayatd dhṛto govardhano nāma saptāhaṃ parvatas tadād śiśunā vāsudevena gavārtham arimardanad krīḍamānas tadā kṛṣṇaḥ kṛtavān karma duṣkaramd tad adbhutam ivātrāsīt sarvalokasya bhāratad devadevaḥ kṣitiṃ gatvā kṛṣṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā mudānvitaḥd govinda iti taṃ hy uktvā hy abhyaṣiñcat puraṃdaraḥd ity uktvāśliṣya govindaṃ puruhūto bhyayād divamd athāriṣṭa iti khyātaṃ daityaṃ vṛṣabhavigrahamd jaghāna tarasā kṛṣṇaḥ paśūnāṃ hitakāmyayād keśinaṃ nāma daiteyaṃ rājan vai hayavigrahamd tathā vanagataṃ pārtha gajāyutabalaṃ hayamd pragṛhya bhojaputrasya jaghāna puruṣottamaḥd āndhraṃ mallaṃ ca cāṇūraṃ nijaghāna mahāsuramd sunāmānam amitraghnaḥ sarvasainyapuraskṛtamd mṛgarūpeṇa govindaṃ trāsayām āsa bhāratad baladevena cāyatnāt samāje muṣṭiko hataḥd trāsitaś ca tadā kaṃsaḥ sa hi kṛṣṇena bhāratad airāvataṃ yuyutsantaṃ mātaṅgānām ivarṣabhamd kṛṣṇaḥ kuvalayāpīḍaṃ hatavāṃs tasya paśyataḥd hatvā kaṃsam amitraghnaḥ sarveṣāṃ paśyatāṃ tadād abhiṣicyograsenaṃ taṃ pitroḥ pādam avandatad evamādīni karmāṇi kṛtavān vai janārdanaḥd bhīṣmaḥd evaṃ bālye pi gopālaiḥ krīḍābhis tau vijahratuḥd tatas tau jagmatus tāta guruṃ sāndīpaniṃ punaḥd guruśuśrūṣayā yuktau dharmajñau dharmacāriṇaud vratam ugraṃ mahātmānau vicarantāv avantiṣud ahorātraiś catuḥṣaṣṭyā ṣaḍaṅgaṃ vedam āpatuḥd lekhyaṃ ca gaṇitaṃ cobhau prāpnutāṃ yadunandanaud gāndharvavedaṃ citraṃ ca sakalaṃ samavāpatuḥd hastiśikṣāśvaśikṣāṃ ca dvādaśāhena cāpatuḥd tāv ubhau jagmatur vīrau guruṃ sāndīpaniṃ punaḥd dhanurvedacikīrṣārthaṃ dharmajñau dharmacāriṇaud tāv iṣvastravarācāryam abhigamya praṇamya cad tena tau satkṛtau rājan vicarantāv avantiṣud pañcāśadbhir ahorātrair daśāṅgaṃ supratiṣṭhitamd sarahasyaṃ dhanurvedaṃ sakalaṃ tāv avāpatuḥd dṛṣṭvā kṛtārthau viprendro gurvarthe tāv acodayatd ayācatārthaṃ govindaṃ tataḥ sāndīpanir vibhuḥd mama putraḥ samudre smiṃs timinā cāpavāhitaḥd putram ānaya bhadraṃ te bhakṣitaṃ timinā mamad ārtāya gurave tatra pratiśuśrāva duṣkaramd aśakyaṃ triṣu lokeṣu kartum anyena kena citd yaś ca sāndīpaneḥ putraṃ jaghāna bharatarṣabhad so suraḥ samare tābhyāṃ samudre vinipātitaḥd tataḥ sāndīpaneḥ putraḥ prasādād amitaujasaḥd dīrghakālaṃ gataḥ pretaḥ punar āsīc charīravānd tad aśakyam acintyaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā sumahad adbhutamd sarveṣām eva bhūtānāṃ vismayaḥ samajāyatad aiśvaryāṇi ca sarvāṇi gavāśvaṃ ca dhanāni cad sarvaṃ tad upajahrāte gurave rāmakeśavaud gadāparighayuddheṣu sarvāstreṣu ca keśavaḥd paramāṃ anyatra puruṣottamātd bhojarājatanūjo pi kaṃsas tāta yudhiṣṭhirad astrajñāne bale vīrye kārtavīryasamo bhavatd tasya bhojapateḥ putrād bhojarājanyavardhanātd udvijante sma rājānaḥ suparṇād iva pannagāḥd citrakārmukanistriṃśavimalaprāsayodhinaḥd śataṃ śatasahasrāṇi pādātās tasya bhāratad aṣṭau śatasahasrāṇi śūrāṇām anivartināmd abhavan bhojarājasya jāmbūnadamayadhvajāḥd rukmakāñcanakakṣyās yudhiṣṭhirad abhavad bhojarājasya dvis tāvad dhi mahad balamd ṣoḍaśāśvasahasrāṇi kiṃśukābhāni tasya vaid aparas tu mahāvyūhaḥ kiśorāṇāṃ yudhiṣṭhirad ārohavarasaṃpanno durdharṣaḥ kena cid balātd sa ca
